Only INCR-15/16/17 add tables вҶ’ **0051/0052/0053** + a `db/sql/prod-paste-005X-*.sql` each. INCR-18/19/20 are read surfaces (don't burn a migration number); INCR-19 adds a **parent-scoped RLS policy** only.

**Portability/RLS (Wells):** tenant tables (composite `(school_id,id)` FKs + `tenant_isolation` FORCE + prod-paste): all `wassce_*` except universities, plus `mock_*`, `university_targets`, `waec_special_consideration`, `readiness_statements`. **Global** (bare ENABLE RLS, never FORCE/tenant_isolation): `universities`, `university_programmes`. **`benchmark_data_points` is MIXED** (`SCHOOLUP_DIRECT`=tenant, `WAEC_NATIONAL/REGIONAL`=global) вҶ’ **lean split-the-table** over nullable-`school_id`-with-conditional-RLS (Kofi/Wells joint call). **No triggers** (best-3 aggregate = pure lib like `compile.ts`; freeze = app-layer; SickbayвҶ’SC-12 auto-suggest deferred to 4.4). **Reuse the portable receipt-PDF path** (#136) for `readiness_statements.parent_signature_pdf_file_id` вҖ” no new PDF dep.

**OWNER calls (surface at module gate; block a *slice*, not the build):** parent-ack SMS provider (same Hubtel gate as 4.2 вҖ” blocks the parent-ack slice of INCR-17/19); university cut-off dataset source (licensed vs school-entered вҖ” blocks uni-match slice of INCR-17/20); benchmark national/region data + multi-school pooling (ship region as `DIRECTIONAL` placeholder; **do NOT build cross-tenant pooling** вҖ” depends on Oversight tier / Phase 5); public mock-accuracy figure (73вҖ“82%) + its update policy; WAEC ICTD API vs printable (build manual/printable path). **No paid-service provisioning needed for the core** (mocks are teacher-entered) вҶ’ no stop-and-ask beyond SMS.

**Cross-module hooks DEFERRED to 4.4 Sickbay / senior backlog (Kofi):** SickbayвҶ’SC-12 auto-suggest (Decision 9) and F3 discipline-pause / WASSCE-window absence-exemption (Decision 6) touch Sickbay (not yet built). INCR-17 ships **SC-12 as manual filing**; auto-suggest is a later app-layer cross-module call (never a trigger).

## Next increment вҖ” INCR-15 В· F0 WASSCE cohort spine В· migration 0051

**Recommended first (Pence):** the sole increment nothing can precede вҖ” every other WASSCE table + all four remaining surfaces FK into `wassce_candidates`/`wassce_subjects`; carries the most schema-shaped Kofi rulings that block Wells; maps to the read-only, lowest-risk part of the setup surface (В§1/В§4/В§5), letting the loop shake out the module's RLS/composite-FK/freeze patterns with no write-side projection math. Exact analogue of 4.2 opening on the HouseвҶ’DormвҶ’Bunk spine.

**Spine tables:** `wassce_programmes вҶ’ wassce_subjects вҶ’ wassce_candidates вҶ’ wassce_papers вҶ’ wassce_paper_sittings` + a per-school **freeze marker** (`wassce_setup_frozen_at`, Decision 1).

**Kofi must rule before Wells designs schema:**
1. **Freeze mechanism (Decision 1):** where `wassce_setup_frozen_at` lives (per-school SHS config row vs per-cohort table), HoA+Headmaster co-sign semantics, which dependent tables lock on freeze, the change-control typo exception. *(WHAT=Kofi, WHERE=Wells.)*
2. **`subjects_sitting_json` vs a normalized `wassce_candidate_subject` join** вҖ” BUILD_STACK says JSON on `wassce_candidates`; repo composite-FK discipline argues for a normalized join with FK integrity to `wassce_subjects`. Kofi call; likely the join table for RLS/FK integrity вҖ” **flag owner if it goes the other way.**
3. **`index_number` uniqueness scope** вҖ” BUILD_STACK writes `UNIQUE(index_number)` (nationally unique WAEC numbers); a *global* unique across tenants leaks row existence + fights isolation. **Flag owner if they choose global** over tenant-scoped.
4. **`wassce_subjects` tenancy** вҖ” must carry `school_id` + composite FK to `wassce_programmes(school_id,id)` so isolation is enforceable (no through-join escape).

**Owner map:** Kofi (rulings + AC for the frozen read-only roster) вҖ– Lucy (`wassce-setup` В§1/В§4/В§5 вҶ’ `docs/senior/wassce-spine-surface-map.md`) вҶ’ Wells (6-table spine + freeze marker + migration 0051 + `prod-paste-0051-wassce-spine.sql`; composite FKs; FORCE RLS) вҶ’ Claude Code (read-only setup/registration surface + apply/verify 0051 on dev + PR) вҶ’ Quinn/Dex/Sarah gates.

**INCR-15 done when:** an SHS admin can view the frozen WASSCE registration roster (programmes, subjects/electives, the candidate list with index numbers, papers/sittings, policy anchors) for the cohort вҖ” tenant-scoped, RLS-enforced, freeze-state signalled, no write-side projection вҖ” three gates green + `prod-paste-0051` ready to hand-paste.

### INCR-15 В· Kofi rulings + AC (2026-07-19) В· Lucy map: `docs/senior/wassce-spine-surface-map.md`
**Spine = 7 tables** (migration 0051): `wassce_cohort` (freeze anchor) вҶ’ `wassce_programmes` вҶ’ `wassce_subjects` вҶ’ `wassce_candidates` вҶ’ **`wassce_candidate_subject`** (join, replaces JSON) вҶ’ `wassce_papers` вҶ’ `wassce_paper_sittings`. All carry `school_id`, composite `(school_id,id)` intra-tenant FKs, `tenant_uk` where referenced, FORCE RLS `tenant_isolation`. INCR-15 is **READ-ONLY** вҖ” seed the WASSCE-2026 F3 cohort already-frozen; **no server action mutates any spine row** (there are none to build).
- **Ruling A** вҖ” schema source = **BUILD_STACK** WASSCE batch (not spec В§4.3's 5-table sketch), amended by 1вҖ“4.
- **Ruling 1 вҖ” freeze is PER-COHORT, keyed `(school_id Г— exam_year)`, NOT a per-school scalar.** The surface shows F3-2026 frozen while F2-2027 stays editable in the same school вҶ’ a scalar can't express that. `wassce_cohort.setup_frozen_at`: NULL = in-flight/editable, non-NULL = frozen. Freeze requires **both** co-signs present: one `HEADMASTER` + one `VICE_HEADMASTER_ACADEMIC` (= Head of Academics in this codebase's `appRoleEnum`; no separate HOA role), each an append-only {actor id, ts}; **self-cosign rejected**. Cohort-scoped rows (candidates, candidate_subject, papers, sittings) lock on freeze; `wassce_programmes`/`wassce_subjects` are durable **school-level** reference (NOT cohort-scoped, edits affect future registrations only). **Typo exception:** post-freeze the ONLY writes are clerical `index_number`/`centre_code` fixes via a co-signed, audit-logged change-control action. **The freeze/unfreeze co-sign action + typo write-flow are DEFERRED** to a later increment вҖ” INCR-15 builds the model + display only.
- **Ruling 2 вҖ” DEVIATION RATIFIED (orchestrator):** replace BUILD_STACK's `wassce_candidates.subjects_sitting_json` with a normalized **`wassce_candidate_subject`** join `(id, school_id, candidate_id, subject_id)`, `UNIQUE(school_id, candidate_id, subject_id)`, composite FKs to candidates + subjects, FORCE RLS. Buys FK integrity + RLS + INCR-18 heatmap `GROUP BY`. `accommodations_json` STAYS json (unstructured SC display).
- **Ruling 3 вҖ” `index_number` = tenant-scoped `UNIQUE(school_id, index_number)`, NOT global.** Centre code is 1:1 with the school (index `0184-0817` = centre `SU-0184` + candidate), so within-school uniqueness already preserves national uniqueness; a global unique leaks cross-tenant row existence below RLS. **No owner escalation** (global was the escalation-worthy option; declined вҖ” future cross-school dup detection = Oversight tier, never a DB constraint).
- **Ruling 4 вҖ” `wassce_subjects` carries `school_id` + composite FK to `wassce_programmes(school_id,id)`** + its own `tenant_uk`; uniform across all 7 tables. Closes the through-join RLS escape.
- **K1** subjects are per-programme rows (no subject-master/join; "23 subjects В· 4 core В· 19 elec" = distinct-display count); `subject_type` `CORE/ELECTIVE/OPTIONAL` вҶ” surface `Core/Elec/Alt`. **K2** `wassce_papers` + `wassce_paper_sittings` are cohort-scoped; sittings `UNIQUE(school_id, candidate_id, paper_id)`. **K3** fee/NHIS/medical are **display flags, never `candidate_status`, never blockers** (Decision 5); `candidate_status_enum` = `REGISTERED/ACTIVE/WITHDRAWN/COMPLETED` (WAEC lifecycle only); INCR-15 seeds these flags as static display (live billing/sickbay reads = later). **K4** `mock_2_aggregate` renders seeded/display-only, `projected_aggregate` stays NULL, tier chips NOT computed (INCR-16/17). **K5** `wassce_programmes`/`wassce_subjects` soft-delete via `active_flag` (never dangle a frozen cohort's reference).

**AC for Quinn** (surface-accurate to `wassce-setup` В§1/В§4/В§5):
- **AВ·cohort/freeze:** seeded F3-2026 cohort `setup_frozen_at` non-NULL with **two distinct** co-sign stamps (HEADMASTER + VICE_HEADMASTER_ACADEMIC); one-stamp fixture вҮ’ NULL; self-cosign rejected; every candidate/subject/paper/sitting resolves to exactly one cohort and inherits its freeze state.
- **BВ·frozen roster (В§4 "the 240"):** no write/edit affordance on frozen rows and **no mutating server action exists**; save-bar shows "Setup is frozen for this cohort"; 240 candidates each render name+student id, programme pill, mono index (`0184-0817`), WAEC reg-status, notes/accommodation, seeded Mock 2 agg; tiles = Confirmed 237/240 В· Flagged 3 В· Accommodations 4 В· fees GHS 336k/0 outstanding; filters All 240В·Sci 60В·Bus 60В·Arts 80В·Home Ec 40; P. Donkor (GHS 240 owing) still REGISTERED/Confirmed; Y. Aidoo (`0184-0817`) "On medical" is display-only (no SC/sickbay write).
- **CВ·matrix (В§1):** 4 programme cards (Sci 60/Bus 60/Arts 80/Home Ec 40) w/ 4 shared cores + electives/alts, tags map `subject_type`; stats strip 240В·4В·23(4 coreВ·19 elec)В·Mocks 2 of 2 (seeded); A1вҖ“F9 band + "best-3-cores+best-3-electives=6вҖҰ54" static.
- **DВ·papers/sittings:** cohort-scoped WAEC-2026 timetable papers (date/time/duration/type/`waec_paper_code`); sittings one-per-(candidateГ—paper) `UNIQUE(school_id,candidate_id,paper_id)`, exemption fields for Y. Aidoo's missed papers, no derivation.
- **EВ·policy (В§5):** WAEC anchors (centre SU-0184, 21 AprвҶ’19 Jun 2026, SC-3/7/12, grading+aggregate) + GES anchors (Free SHS GHS 1,400/candidate, "no candidate denied for fees" as TEXT only вҖ” no fee-gating code path).
- **FВ·isolation:** all 7 tables FORCE RLS + `prod-paste-0051` mirrors dev policies; a second school SELECTs zero cohort rows; every intra-tenant FK composite (mismatched `school_id` insert rejected); `index_number` unique is `(school_id, index_number)` вҖ” two schools, no collision/no cross-tenant error.
- **GВ·no projection leak:** module imports no mock/projection/`compile`/best-3 logic; `mock_2_aggregate` seeded-only, `projected_aggregate` NULL/unused; university tier band NOT computed (seeded/static or omitted).

**Lucy map + binding gaps (render seeded/static/inert, NOT computed or wired):** Mock 2 agg column + Aggregate sort + "Mocks 2 of 2" (INCR-16/17 вҶ’ em-dash/omit; disable Aggregate sort); live-exam banner (static or defer); A1вҖ“F9 + SC-form list + GES anchors = `lib/wassce/` constants, not tables; billing figures = static `count Г— GHS 1,400` (cross-module Billing); Sickbay/VLC referral cards = static from a candidate flag (4.4/4.5 unbuilt); Gen. Arts `#7B4A8A` = per-programme inline color (not a token, mirrors boarding House-hex drift вҖ” no slash-opacity); centre code `SU-0184` = per-school WASSCE config, not a spine table. **WRITE controls to render INERT (contradict read-only, do NOT build):** `Edit В· F2 cohort`, `+ Late registration`, any freeze/unfreeze toggle, nav-out buttons to unbuilt targets. Export/Print/Audit-history are reads (safe to wire/stub); filter/sort pills are client view-state (safe; disable Aggregate sort). **No-alpha discipline:** every `rgba()` in scope вҶ’ arbitrary-rgba or `opacity-N`, never `bg-gold/8`.

**Orchestrator ratifications (no owner call needed for INCR-15):** Ruling 2 join-over-JSON **RATIFIED**; co-sign order = both-present/order-agnostic (Kofi), UX default HoA-proposesвҶ’Headmaster-ratifies, not enforced, write-flow deferred; Ruling 3 tenant-scoped, no escalation.

Slightly exceeds R3b's config-only wording вҖ” **note to Kofi** (non-blocking).

  1. **Quinn obs вҖ” write-path integrity (INCR-18):** `saveMockResult` verifies candidateвҲҲcohort + subject-exists but NOT that the candidate is REGISTERED for that `wassce_subject` (via `wassce_candidate_subject`). ### INCR-17 В· Kofi rulings + AC (2026-07-19)
**SPLIT CONFIRMED (domain-sound):** the readiness statement does NOT require the university match (BUILD_STACK gives `university_targets` its OWN `parent_acknowledged_at`, separate from `readiness_statements`). **INCR-17 (0053):** `projectAggregate` pure lib + `waec_special_consideration` + `readiness_statements` (academic core; `target_universities_json` NULL). **INCR-17b (0054):** `universities`/`university_programmes`/`university_targets` + wassce-setup В§3 + В§6 match + per-target ack. **New tables (0053):** `waec_special_consideration` (TENANT, leaf), `readiness_statements` (TENANT, references `mock_exams`). **Enums:** `sc_form_enum` (SC-3/SC-7/SC-12), `sc_status_enum` (DRAFT/FILED/ACKNOWLEDGED/APPROVED/SCHEDULED/COMPLETED/REJECTED), `parent_ack_method_enum` (PHONE_OTP/IN_PERSON/PDF_UPLOAD). NOT enums: readiness state = **derived** from `parent_acknowledged_at`+`superseded_at`; `projected_band` = text label (lib `bandForAggregate()`). Deferred to 17b: `university_type_enum`, `target_rank_enum`. `wassce_results` (post-release actuals) **DEFERRED** entirely.

**рҹ”‘ THE PROJECTION ALGORITHM (`lib/wassce/projection.ts`, pure lib, NO trigger вҖ” crown jewel):**
- Partition by `subject_type`: **COREвҶ’core pool; ELECTIVE or OPTIONALвҶ’elective pool** (OPTIONAL/"Alt" competes in best-3-electives). Per-subject grade = predictor mock's `COALESCE(moderated_grade, grade)` (reuse `effectiveGrade`); `gradePoints = gradeOrdinal+1` (A1=1вҖҰF9=9).
- If вүҘ3 graded cores AND вүҘ3 graded electives вҶ’ sort each pool by **`(points asc, name asc)`** (deterministic tie-break), counted = first 3, dropped = rest (dropped stays rendered at `opacity-45`, never filtered). `aggregate = ОЈ points of the 6 counted` вҖ” **includes D7/E8/F9** (min 6 = six A1, max 54 = six F9). `band = bandForAggregate(aggregate)`.
- If `<3` in either pool вҶ’ **`{computable:false, reason: INSUFFICIENT_CORES|INSUFFICIENT_ELECTIVES}`** вҖ” NEVER a partial 5-subject number (would misread vs cut-offs). `isCredit` (A1вҖ“C6) is a SEPARATE per-subject flag, NOT a filter on the aggregate sum (six F9 вҶ’ agg 54, 0 credits).
- **Canonical fixture Y. Aidoo = 10:** cores IntSci A1/Math B2/Eng B3/Social B3 вҶ’ keep IntSci+Math+Eng=6, **drop Social** (ties Eng at 3; "English Language" < "Social Studies" вҶ’ English kept, matches В§5 exactly); electives Bio A1/Chem A1/Phys B2/ElecMath C4 вҶ’ keep Bio+Chem+Phys=4. Agg=10. Ship a runnable self-check (fixture=10, all-A1=6, all-F9=54, tie-break drops Social, <3 coresвҶ’not-computable, exempted-live-paper input = same number).
- **Decision 11 medical HOLD = STRUCTURAL:** `projectAggregate` reads ONLY the predictor mock, **never `wassce_paper_sittings`** вҖ” a missed/exempted live paper (SC-12) cannot affect the number (Mock 2 was sat in March, pre-disruption). No `if(medical)` branch. If Mock 2 ITSELF is incomplete вҶ’ that's the 1(c) partial-data NULL, not a Decision-11 case.
- **STORED vs DERIVED (hybrid):** live aggregate = **DERIVED-on-read** via the pure lib (no drift, no trigger, `compile.ts` idiom); `wassce_candidates.projected_aggregate` stays **NULL in the live path**; the ONLY stored copy is the **immutable frozen snapshot on `readiness_statements`**. `projected_aggregate == mock_2_aggregate` in INCR-17 (no trajectory-based numeric adjustment вҖ” trajectory is context narrative only; a numeric adjust would be the "hidden logic" Decision 12 forbids). **Cleanup (Claude Code):** point the roster's Mock-2-agg column at the DERIVED value, don't trust the INCR-15 seeded static (one source of truth).
- **OWNER-ESCALATE (non-blocking):** pure best-3-of-4-cores (spec/surface/visualizer-accurate) vs the real Ghana university-ADMISSION rule (English + Core Maths mandatory, best-of the rest as 3rd core). Diverge ONLY when Eng/Maths is a candidate's WORST core (not in the Y. Aidoo demo). **Ship pure best-3 now; flag the Eng/Maths refinement to owner tied to 17b** (where cut-off matching makes admission-accurate aggregates load-bearing). Projection number is advisory, never WAEC-authoritative.

**Ruling 3 вҖ” SC-form (`waec_special_consideration`, WRITE surface, manual filing):** SC-3 (pre-exam sensory/physical accommodations), SC-7 (chronic-condition extra time), SC-12 (in-window medical disruption/missed papers). Shape: `school_id`, composite FK `(school_id, candidate_id)`, `sc_form`, `status`, `filed_at`, `filed_by_user_id`(SET NULL), nullable `medical_cert_file_id`/`clinician_letter_file_id` (stay NULL вҖ” no file layer), `waec_acknowledged_at`, `waec_ref`, `approved_at`, `make_up_scheduled_at`, `make_up_centre`, `completed_at`, `notes`. **UNIQUE(school_id, candidate_id, sc_form)** (refile updates). TENANT, FORCE RLS, LEAF, mutable workflow. Gated to `WASSCE_SETUP_ROLES` (no new exams-officer/matron role). SickbayвҶ’SC-12 auto-suggest DEFERRED to 4.4. Setup В§5 SC list stays policy-display (a `lib/wassce` constant); the real filing artifact is on student-readiness.

**Ruling 4 вҖ” readiness statement (`readiness_statements`, frozen artifact):** cols `school_id`, composite FK `(school_id, candidate_id)`, `mock_2_id` composite FK `(school_id, mock_2_id)`вҶ’`mock_exams`, `projected_aggregate`(frozen), `projected_band`(frozen text), **`projection_snapshot_json` jsonb** (`{mock1Aggregate, mock2Aggregate, projectedAggregate, band, subjects:[{name,type,grade,points,counted}]}` вҖ” the В§5 visualizer + Mock1вҶ’Mock2 trajectory frozen), `target_universities_json` **NULL (17b)**, `generated_at`, `generated_by_user_id`(SET NULL), `superseded_at` NULL, parent-ack: `parent_acknowledged_at`, `parent_acknowledged_signature_method`(enum), `parent_acknowledged_phone`, `parent_concerns_text`, `parent_signature_pdf_file_id`(NULL). **Generation:** manual by `WASSCE_SETUP_ROLES`, gated on predictor `marking_complete_at IS NOT NULL` AND computable; lib runs ONCE, output frozen. **Regeneration supersedes** (new row + prior `superseded_at`; state derived, no status enum). **Parent-ack in INCR-17 = SCHOOL-CAPTURED** (HoA records the ack; the parent-facing signing UI is INCR-19). **PDF = reuse #136 trio** (`lib/pdf/readiness-statement-document.tsx` + `render-readiness-statement.tsx` + `app/api/senior/readiness-statement/[id]/route.ts`, `runtime="nodejs"`, RLS-scoped, `renderToBuffer`, on-demand render вҖ” NO new dep, NO files table, re-render from the frozen snapshot). **Parent-ack SMS = OWNER-GATED console-degrade** via existing `sendSms()` (same Hubtel gate as boarding вҖ” NEVER provision creds; console-OTP or IN_PERSON keeps it testable).

**AC (Quinn):** AC1 Y.AidooвҶ’10 (cores {IntSci,Math,Eng} drop Social, electives {Bio,Chem,Phys} drop ElecMath) В· AC2 six-A1=6, six-F9=54, D7вҖ“F9 summed В· AC3 six-F9вҶ’agg 54/credit 0 (isCreditвү aggregate filter) В· AC4 OPTIONAL pools with electives В· AC5 (points asc,name asc) deterministic tie-break В· AC6 <3 either poolвҶ’not-computable, generation blocked В· AC7 predictor `effectiveGrade` only, Mock1 never feeds agg В· AC8 **medical HOLD** вҖ” exempted-live-paper candidate = identical agg, no sitting-table read В· AC9 derived/no-trigger/no-drift, `projected_aggregate` NULL live path В· AC10 SC-form CRUD+states, `UNIQUE(school_id,candidate_id,sc_form)` В· AC11 SC authz `WASSCE_SETUP_ROLES` (teacher rejected), composite FK В· AC12 statement freezes agg/band/snapshot, later moderation doesn't change it В· AC13 generation gate (marking_complete_at + computable), `mock_2_id` set В· AC14 regen supersedes (new row + `superseded_at`, derived state) В· AC15 parent-ack method/at/phone/concerns, SMS **console-degrades** (no creds read) В· AC16 PDF via #136 (no new dep, university block omitted) В· AC17 **no university leak** (no universities/targets/cut-off/tier, `target_universities_json` NULL) В· AC18 no `wassce_results` read/write В· AC19 tenant isolation (both tables FORCE, composite FKs, prod-paste-0053) В· AC20 Dex NIT-1 done (`mock-data.ts:388,393`вҶ’`isDistinction`/`isCredit`).

### INCR-17b В· Kofi rulings + AC (2026-07-19)
**рҹ”‘ KEY INSIGHT:** the В§6 headline candidate aggregate (`10`) is the SAME number in every tile; **TARGET is NOT a computed band вҖ” it's the PRIMARY-CHOICE overlay.** The 4 *computed* bands are SAFETY/COMFORTABLE/MATCH/STRETCH; a FIRST_CHOICE target always renders **TARGET** regardless of its computed band. This reproduces the В§6 header "1 target В· 1 comfortable В· 2 stretch В· 1 safety" exactly and explains why NO tile shows MATCH (the only Оҙ+1 programme is the primary вҶ’ TARGET).
**New tables (0054):** `universities` (**GLOBAL**, bare ENABLE RLS), `university_programmes` (**GLOBAL**, bare ENABLE RLS), `university_targets` (**TENANT**, FORCE RLS). Enums: **`university_type`** (PUBLIC_UNIVERSITY/PRIVATE_UNIVERSITY/TECHNICAL_UNIVERSITY/POLYTECHNIC/NURSING_COLLEGE/EDUCATION_COLLEGE), **`target_rank`** (**AMENDED to** FIRST_CHOICE/SECOND_CHOICE/THIRD_CHOICE вҖ” the stretch/match/safety words are the *computed* band, so storing them too = two sources of truth; nullable). **NO `match_tier` enum** вҖ” the 5-tier band is a DERIVED lib label.
- **R1 tables/tenancy:** `universities` (global: name, short_name, `university_type`, location, region) вҖ” single-col FKs only. `university_programmes` (global: single-col FKвҶ’universities RESTRICT, name, qualification, duration_years, `current_cut_off` smallint CHECK 6..54, `cut_off_reference_year` NOT NULL, `cut_off_history_json`, `prerequisite_subjects_json`) вҖ” **seed-only in 17b, no update UI** (dropped BUILD_STACK `updated_*`/`public_or_private`/`accreditation_status` вҖ” YAGNI). `university_targets` (tenant: **composite `(school_id,candidate_id)`вҶ’wassce_candidates**, single-col `university_programme_id`вҶ’programmes RESTRICT, `target_rank` nullable, `tagged_by_user_id` SET NULL, `parent_acknowledged_at` [column now, no writer], notes) В· `UNIQUE(school_id,candidate_id,university_programme_id)` В· **partial `UNIQUE(school_id,candidate_id,target_rank) WHERE target_rank IS NOT NULL`** (one FIRST/SECOND/THIRD per candidate).
- **R2 match function (pure lib `lib/wassce/university-match.ts`, no trigger, derived-on-read, NOT stored):** `Оҙ = cutOff вҲ’ projected` (lower agg = stronger; cutOff = worst admitted). `matchBand`: ОҙвүҘ+4 SAFETY В· ОҙвүҘ+2 COMFORTABLE В· ОҙвүҘвҲ’1 MATCH В· else STRETCH (total, non-overlapping). `matchTier(proj,cut,isPrimary) = isPrimary ? "TARGET" : matchBand`; `isPrimary = target_rank==="FIRST_CHOICE"`. `matchMargin` вҶ’ {inside/outside/on, |Оҙ|}. Only called when `projectAggregate` is computable (else "projection pending", no bands). Legend copy overlaps (editorial) вҖ” **tile values are ground truth**.
- **R3 AGGREGATE вҖ” DECIDED: single pure best-3** (no admission-accurate variant). В§5 and В§6 show ONE number; Y. Aidoo identical under both rules; projection is advisory not WAEC-authoritative. The English+Core-Maths admission concern is folded into **prerequisites** (R6), not a 2nd aggregate. `ponytail:` residual bias (weak-but-credit English/Maths as worst core = slightly optimistic) bounded by the credit-prereq check. **OWNER-CONFIRM non-blocking** вҖ” recommend defer the `admissionAggregate()` variant to v2.
- **R4 `target_universities_json` freeze:** the В§6 board is LIVE/derive-on-read; the statement's `target_universities_json` is FROZEN only at statement (re)generation (mirrors INCR-17 `projection_snapshot_json`). Target CRUD writes `university_targets` ONLY вҖ” never supersedes/regenerates a statement. Generation snapshots current live targets + computed match; regeneration supersedes + re-snapshots; a no-target generation writes `[]` (vs legacy INCR-17 NULL). Frozen element: `{universityName,shortName,universityType,programmeName,qualification,location,cutOff,cutOffReferenceYear,targetRank,isPrimary,projectedAggregate,matchBand,displayTier,margin,prerequisites}`.
- **R5 per-target parent-ack:** column authored now, **write-flow DEFERRED to INCR-19** вҖ” the В§7 ack is ONE bundled statement-level ack (INCR-17's `readiness_statements.parent_acknowledged_at`), not per-programme.
- **R6 prerequisites вҖ” modeled + CHECKED (not display-only):** `university_programmes.prerequisite_subjects_json` = `[{subject,minGrade}|{anyOf:[вҖҰ],minGrade}]` (grounds "Physics OR Elec Math"). `checkPrerequisites(rules, effectiveGrades, registered)` (pure lib) вҶ’ {met, unmet[], pending[]}: satisfied = registered via `wassce_candidate_subject` AND predictor `effectiveGrade` credit вүҘ minGrade; `pending` = registered/no grade; `unmet` = below-credit or not-registered. **Universal seed baseline: every programme requires English вүҘ C6 + Core Maths вүҘ C6** (encodes the admission concern in DATA). `ponytail:` subject name-match seam (same as INCR-16 FORWARD-1) вҖ” upgrade to a per-school alias/FK if vocabularies drift; flag, don't build.
- **Portability:** match+prereq = pure lib (no trigger); universities/programmes GLOBAL (bare ENABLE RLS, GLOBAL block of policies.sql + prod-paste-0054, seed-only); `university_targets` TENANT (FORCE, prod-paste-0054 hand-paste); composite tenant FK on targets, single-col to global programme + SET NULL actor. **Kofi owns the BUILD_STACK sync** (target_rank values, the column trims, "band is derived") once 0054 lands.

**AC (Quinn):** AC1 `matchBand(10,В·)`=SAFETY@14/COMFORTABLE@12/MATCH@11/STRETCH@8/STRETCH@6 В· AC2 `matchTier(10,11,primary)`=TARGET, `(вҖҰ,false)`=MATCH В· AC3 boundaries total/non-overlapping (Оҙ +4вҶ’SAFETY,+3вҶ’COMF,+2вҶ’COMF,+1вҶ’MATCH,0вҶ’MATCH,вҲ’1вҶ’MATCH,вҲ’2вҶ’STRETCH) В· AC4 tally reproduces В§6 header (1 primary + 4 computed, NO MATCH tile) В· AC5 margins 1in/2in/2out/4out/4in В· AC6 not-computable вҶ’ "projection pending", no bands В· AC7 В§6 "YouВ·N" == В§5 headline (single aggregate; Y. Aidoo 10) В· AC8 universities/programmes GLOBAL bare-ENABLE (no FORCE/no school_id, Data-API-denied) В· AC9 `university_targets` TENANT fail-closed, composite-FK cross-tenant impossible В· AC10 FKs compositeвҶ’candidates + single-col RESTRICTвҶ’programmes В· AC11 target CRUD gated `WASSCE_SETUP_ROLES` (teacher rejected; universities/programmes read-only to schools) В· AC12 dup-programme + 2nd-FIRST_CHOICE rejected, NULL-rank multiple allowed В· AC13 target edit does NOT create/supersede a statement В· AC14 generation snapshots targets+match into `target_universities_json`, regen supersedes+re-snapshots, no-targetвҶ’`[]` В· AC15 frozen json unchanged by later cut-off/target edits (live board reflects them) В· AC16 `checkPrerequisites` met/unmet/pending (Y. ## вң… MERGED (PR #164, `54e2b1f`+`fb139ec`) вҖ” repo-wide 23505 retrofit В· no schema, no prod-paste
The queued retrofit is **DONE** (it is no longer pending вҖ” Kofi's INCR-18 note to "fold it in" predates the merge). Probing a real duplicate insert proved Drizzle wraps every driver failure: thrown `.code` is `undefined` and thrown `.message` is only `"Failed query: вҖҰ"`, while the real `PostgresError` (`code`, `constraint_name`) hangs off `.cause`. So BOTH idioms in the repo were dead: `(err as {code?}).code === "23505"` AND `String(err.message).includes("duplicate key")`. All 8 sites revived. Two were live user-facing defects: `boarding-exeat.ts` (the check guards a ref-code **retry loop** вҶ’ retry was dead code, exeat creation hard-threw on any collision) and `boarding.ts` (a lost bunk race **threw** instead of returning "just taken"). Extracted the classifier to a PURE `lib/db/pg-error.ts` (re-exported from `rls.ts`, zero call-site import changes) + **8 regression tests** pinning the real wrapper shape вҖ” this class is invisible to build/typecheck/lint. Post-review (Quinn): the whatsapp constraint is `uniq_whatsapp_template_name_per_school` (the old code matched by SUBSTRING; `===` silently killed that branch), and the bare `|| code === "23505"` fallback was dropped from `onboarding.ts` (that tx also creates classes/subjects/roles/fees, so an unrelated dupe was reported as a GES-code clash). Every constraint literal in `lib/` swept against `pg_constraint` + `pg_indexes` вҖ” all present (`uniq_student_current_bunk`, `uniq_university_target_rank` are partial unique INDEXES, which postgres.js still reports via `constraint_name`). Also shipped `docs/OWNER-TODO.md` (owner-assigned pre-go-live actions).

(5) **Sarah NIT** free-text reason stored twice вҶ’ once on `audit_log.reason`; also dropped the prior reason from `before` on the same reasoning (it lives on the prior moderation's own audit row).
- **Three omissions ADJUDICATED (Quinn):** C.8 vocabulary card **justified** (defines "Resolved", a status the system cannot enter once case-management was cut вҖ” exactly the AC22 failure mode). D.4 cross-module strip **justified and it OVERRIDES Lucy's map** вҖ” its Sickbay card asserts live wiring to unbuilt module 4.4 and the VLC card hard-codes a student's state that contradicts her real dev state; **AC22 outranks the map on conflict вҖ” logged here as a deliberate map deviation so it is not silently re-added.** C.9 no-targets guard **not an under-build** вҖ” the board ratified `atRisk = reasons.length > 0` with no guard and the implementer followed it; overturning needs a Kofi ruling, not a QA finding.
- **рҹҹ  Deferred (forward-looking):** the merge rests on an invariant the schema does not enforce (`uniq_wassce_candidate_subject` is keyed on `subject_id`, not name) вҖ” zero occurrences today; when R9's `ledger_subject_id` lands, re-key the merge to it. When a registration UI is built, constrain the subject picker to the candidate's programme (that is the guard keeping this merge exact). Cohort-scoping the driving query at the index becomes worthwhile past ~3 archived cohorts.
- **рҹ”ҙ RECOMMENDED NEXT INCREMENT вҖ” pre-existing privilege escalation in `lib/auth` (Sarah HIGH, NOT an INCR-18 defect):** `lib/auth/index.ts:185-196` builds `AppUser.roles` from **every** role assignment at **any** school, and `lib/auth/server.ts:64-71` picks the active school as an unordered `LIMIT 1`. So a user who is TEACHER at School A and ADMIN at School B carries `"ADMIN"` while operating at School A вҖ” passing `requireSchoolRole(WASSCE_SETUP_ROLES)` AND `assertAnyRole(...)` there, enough to read School A's whole-cohort PII dashboard and moderate School A grades. **NOT a cross-tenant leak** (RLS holds; the active school is not attacker-selectable) and `lib/auth/` is untouched by this diff вҖ” but it is the **ceiling on INCR-18's headline authz guarantee** and **every `requireSchoolRole`/`assertAnyRole` site repo-wide inherits it**. Fix in ONE place: scope roles to the active school (`rolesFor(schoolId)`, thread `school.id` into `assertAnyRole`). Record R8 as "hard-denied for single-school users" until it lands.

## рҹ”җ AUTH FIX (PR #167 вҖ” awaiting owner merge) В· no schema, no migration, no prod-paste
Taken BEFORE INCR-19 at the owner's direction, closing the privilege escalation Sarah found gating INCR-18. **Three defects, one root cause вҖ” the role query constrained neither school nor time.** Proved against the DB with a synthetic multi-school user (rolled back), running the OLD query shape first as a negative control: old вҶ’ active school **B** (arbitrary вҖ” unordered) with roles `[ADMIN@B, HEADMASTER@A(ended 2019-12-31), TEACHER@A]`; new вҶ’ active **A**, roles `[TEACHER]`.
- **(1) cross-school union** вҶ’ roles scoped to the active school. **(2) expired assignments still granted roles** (`end_date` documented "null = currently active"; nothing enforced it, so departed staff kept every permission). **(3) non-deterministic active school** вҖ” and `getActiveSchool` ran a SECOND independent unordered query, so it could resolve a different school than the roles came from.
- **Fixed at the SOURCE, not the ~129 `hasAnyRole`/`assertAnyRole`/`requireSchoolRole` sites across ~41 files.** Threading a school id through them makes the property a per-call-site obligation with 129 chances to forget вҖ” and the 130th starts at zero. `AppUser.roles` is now BY CONSTRUCTION only the active school's roles, so every existing AND future check inherits the correction. Dex verified the premise: `AppUser` has exactly **two** constructors, both in `lib/auth/index.ts`; the invariant is documented on the field itself where a future identity-path author (impersonation / service account / `getUserById`) will read it.
- **The time window is now testable.** It lived only in a drizzle WHERE clause no test could reach вҖ” mistyping `gte(endDate, today)` as `gt` would lock out every staff member whose assignment ends today and leave the suite green (Quinn MINOR-1). `isCurrentlyActive(start,end,today)` is now a pure predicate and the AUTHORITY (`scopeRolesToActiveSchool` re-applies it; SQL is a pre-filter). **Mutation-checked** вҖ” that exact typo fails 2 of the new tests.
- **Also fixed from the gate:** `getActiveSchool` now takes the already-resolved user (my original commit claimed the divergence was "structurally impossible" вҖ” it wasn't, so it was fixed rather than reworded); and **`AUTH_DEV_BYPASS` defaulted to `true`, i.e. the auth kill-switch FAILED OPEN** вҖ” absent/misspelled on prod, `authIsLive()` goes false even with Supabase configured, every request becomes `DEV_USER` with `["ADMIN"]` at a real school. Now `.default("false")`; every documented path sets it explicitly so only the forgot-it case changes, and that case must deny.
- **Gates ALL GREEN:** Sarah **CLEAR-TO-MERGE** (26/26 probe assertions; negative control on the old query). Quinn **GREEN** (all 5 dev users byte-identical before/after; 6/6 date boundaries; `getActiveSchool` JSON-identical shape; dev-bypass live-verified with HTTP 200s on every gated senior surface). Dex **APPROVE** (proved purity by BUNDLING `roles.ts` вҖ” 403 bytes, one input, zero runtime deps вҖ” noting the green suite alone was NOT proof since `lib/env.ts` never throws). 444 tests В· typecheck В· lint В· clean build exit 0.
- **вҡ пёҸ DEPLOY:** any prod `role_assignment` row with a stale `end_date` **loses access the moment this ships** вҖ” correct, but it will look like an outage. Count first. Dev has zero, and no app path writes `end_date`, so the blast radius is hand-imported data only. Second note: the app computes `today` in UTC while Postgres writes `start_date` with the DB session TimeZone вҖ” fine on UTC/Accra, but a session east of UTC could briefly lock out a new starter.
- **INTENDED denial (a behaviour change, not a no-op):** a user whose assignments have ALL ended now gets no school and lands on `/start` instead of a working session. That is the bug being fixed; zero users affected on dev.
- **рҹҹ  Follow-ups raised, deliberately NOT in the PR:** (a) **`role_assignment.scope_ref` is DEAD SCHEMA** вҖ” declared as scoping a role to programme/house/class, read by NOTHING; real narrowing happens via domain tables (`house.hm_user_id`, `senior_subject_teacher`), which is the better design. Risk is the INVERSE of unenforcement вҖ” someone will *read* it believing it's populated. Drop it or fix the comment (Wells). (b) **Three definitions of "active assignment" now coexist** вҖ” auth (correct), `isNull(end)` in `lib/reports/school-stats-data.ts:188`, `endDate === null` in `app/(app)/staff/[id]/page.tsx:182`, plus no window at all on the staff roster/dashboard headcount; visible symptom is a departed staffer listed while auth correctly grants them nothing. (c) A **school switcher** вҖ” active school is deterministic but not user-selectable; deliberate (security correction, not a feature), seam is `scopeRolesToActiveSchool(assignments, preferredSchoolId?)`. (d) `resolveActor` attributes audit rows to `roles[0]` вҖ” now deterministic but still arbitrary, not "most privileged".

**OWNER notes (non-blocking):** (1) a true "% projected to qualify" metric is **omitted** вҖ” the honest cohort signal is the all-credit tile; if wanted it must be the Ghana tertiary-entry rule (credits in Eng + Core Maths + Int Sci/Social + 3 electives) and is better placed on the post-release actuals path (`wassce_results`, deferred). (2) **рҹ“Ң SCOPE GAP:** the surface's **"Live exam tracker"** page has **no increment anywhere in INCR-15вҶ’20** вҖ” flag to the owner as a missing planned surface; INCR-18 must NOT absorb it. (3) Part E moderation copy is NEW (not in any surface) вҶ’ owner sign-off. (4) Kofi owns a BUILD_STACK sync post-merge (Decision 10 still names `*_staff_id` and omits `moderated_grade`/`moderation_reason`).

## рҹ”ҙ INCR-19 В· Parent-tracker вҖ” RE-PLAN REQUIRED (board row was wrong on all 3 counts)

The board planned INCR-19 as *"none new; parent-scoped RLS policy (prod-paste); parent-facing capstone (read-only, one child)"*. **Not buildable as written.** Pence found one blocker; Kofi verified it and found three more; Lucy corroborated independently from the surface side. **No code written вҖ” awaiting owner steer on the claiming flow.**

### The five blockers
1. **No parentвҶ’student linkage exists anywhere.** `student_guardian` (`db/schema/students.ts:196`) is SMS-contact data only (`name`/`relationship`/`phone`/`email`/`is_primary`) вҖ” **no `user_id`**. `lib/actions/invites.ts` greps zero for `studentId|PARENT`; `invite.assignments` jsonb is *teacher* class grants. `PARENT` appears ONLY as an enum member, in `NON_STAFF_ROLE_CODES`, and in tests asserting it is DENIED вҖ” **the role has never granted anything.** INCR-19 would be the first surface a parent can reach.
2. **рҹ”ҙ Per-user RLS does not exist (the biggest under-estimate).** `withSchool` (`lib/db/rls.ts:10-18`) sets exactly ONE GUC, `app.current_school`; every policy is generated as `school_id = current_setting('app.current_school')` (`policies.sql:149-153`). **RLS can see WHICH SCHOOL is asking, never WHICH USER.** So "parent-scoped RLS policy (prod-paste)" is not a paste вҖ” it is a change to the seam every tenant read passes through. Getting it backwards "either locks staff out of every table or opens every row" (Kofi).
3. **The surface's data spine is partly unbuilt.** В§1 hero (Ward B bed 7, IV artesunate, Dr Nyarko, 14:30 ward round), the Hospital card and the NHIS card all read **Sickbay вҖ” module 4.4, NOT BUILT**. No sickbay table exists (the only `SICKBAY` in schema is a *prefect role*); `student_health_record` has no NHIS/ward/clinician. В§4's phone-call events are unrepresentable вҖ” `inbox_message` is SMS/WhatsApp-only. **"Shipping a hardcoded hospital bed to a real mother is the worst failure available in this module."**
4. **рҹ”ҙ BLOCKING surface gap (Lucy):** В§3 step 3 **"Awaiting fit-to-sit"** вҖ” the pulsing ACTIVE step, the most prominent element in the section вҖ” **maps to no `sc_status` value and its date is stored nowhere**. `REJECTED` has no parent-facing design at all.
5. **Comms has no store:** `notification_log` is SMS-only вҖ” 3 of 6 thread rows and 5 of 7 per-row fields (channel, from-label, direction, duration, scheduled-future) have no columns.

### Kofi's rulings
- **R1 LINKAGE = `student_guardian.user_id`** (nullable, **single-column** FK вҶ’ `ref_user` `ON DELETE SET NULL` вҖ” `ref_user` is GLOBAL so composite doesn't apply). Migration **0055**. **Phone-match REJECTED OUTRIGHT** (not on balance): shared family SIMs are normal in Ghana (the demo's own Aidoo household), MTN recycles numbers, and `normalizeGhanaPhone` returns raw input on unrecognised shapes вҖ” so "equal phone" is not even a stable relation. A separate `parent_student` table also rejected: `student_guardian` already IS the relation (it carries `relationship`/`is_primary`), and a second table drifts the dangerous way вҖ” **a guardian removed from contacts would keep portal access**.
- **R2 CLAIMING = school-issued, PER-CHILD invite + OTP to the STORED number** рҹ”¶ **OWNER-ESCALATE** (genuinely a product decision; specs are silent вҖ” BUILD_STACK Decision 13 says only "a parent-scoped role"). Add a real `invite.student_id` **column** (not the untyped jsonb) + composite `(school_id, student_id)` FK. Staff pick a `student_guardian` row вҶ’ invite; guardian opens token (factor 1) вҶ’ OTP to `student_guardian.phone` **as stored** (factor 2). **What stops someone claiming another child by typing that guardian's number: NOTHING IS TYPED.** Siblings need their own invite deliberately (auto-linking rows sharing a phone re-imports the phone boundary at claim time). Self-serve REJECTED вҖ” it lets anyone enumerate which numbers are guardians at which school; if the owner wants it, required mitigations are OTP-to-stored-number-only + a school-side approval queue. **SMS console-degrades; never provision `HUBTEL_*`.**
- **R3 VISIBILITY** вҖ” allowed: child card, candidate status + SC-12 state, that candidate's 9 papers, the SC-12 row's public fields, comms where `contact_phone` is this parent's own, the CURRENT (non-superseded) readiness statement + PDF, static FAQ. **Hard denials (query-layer, not page-level):** any other candidate anywhere; ALL cohort data (`benchmark_*`, INCR-18 aggregates, distributions, rank, percentile, "N of 240"); the **moderation trail** (parent sees the effective grade ONLY via the frozen snapshot, never a live `mock_results` row); at-risk internals + `reg_flag`; **superseded statements**; `audit_log`; `waec_special_consideration.notes`/`filed_by_user_id` (staff free text); other guardians' rows; the existence of any other student. **OMIT don't fake** the Sickbay hero/NHIS/call-log (INCR-17 precedent: omitted, not placeholdered). **A `DRAFT` SC-12 must NOT be shown** (Lucy вҖ” the school hasn't filed; showing it promises something that hasn't happened).
- **R4 NO PARENT WRITE PATH.** The surface settles it: В§5 is titled *"what you signed in March"* and its notes read *"End the parent view with reassurance, not action."* Lucy inventoried all 11 interactive elements вҖ” **zero forms/inputs/buttons/signature/OTP/reply/upload**; OTP appears only as past-tense provenance. **The parent-facing signing UI (INCR-17 R4) is DESCOPED вҶ’ senior backlog** (no surface exists for the March signing moment; do not invent one). **INCR-17b R5 per-target ack stays unwritten** вҖ” keep the column, document "no writer, by ruling". рҹ”¶ **OWNER-ESCALATE (honesty):** `parent_acknowledged_signature_method = PHONE_OTP` is *recorded by staff*, NOT *proven by a challenge*, yet В§5 renders it as if cryptographic вҖ” recommend softening the parent copy to "acknowledgement recorded by the school В· confirmed by phone" NOW, and building real OTP signing later as its own increment.
- **R5 SPLIT вҖ” YES.** **19a** = linkage + claiming + **the per-user RLS mechanism** + deny suite В· migration 0055 В· **no surface** В· gated on **Sarah**. **19b** = the read-only surface. **Route-group rule:** build the portal as its own `app/(parent)/вҖҰ` with its own layout вҖ” **never admit a PARENT into `app/(app)/`** (that shell assumes staff: sidebar, `/start`, finance redirects).
- **R6 Г— PR #167** вҖ” model works (PARENT is in NO role group in `lib/access.ts`, so all ~129 gates fail closed; #167 also stops parent roles unioning across schools). **Caveat:** a parent with children at two schools gets the earliest-claimed school **permanently** вҖ” fails closed and leaks nothing, but is not acceptable product behaviour, so the portal **must SAY SO** ("children at more than one school; contact the school") rather than render one child as the whole picture. **Gap вҖ” revocation:** nothing ends a parent's `role_assignment`; therefore **entitlement derives from the LIVE guardian link, not the role assignment** вҖ” deleting the guardian row revokes access in the same statement. рҹ”¶ OWNER-ESCALATE: retention after graduation (note the trap вҖ” a WASSCE candidate graduates in the same window the results land).
- **RLS mechanism вҖ” RULED (i) second GUC.** Add `withParentScope(schoolId, userId)` setting `app.current_school` AND `app.current_parent_user`; generate a `parent_isolation` policy family (expressed ONCE like `tenant_isolation` at `policies.sql:149`, not bespoke per table) restricting rows to students linked via `student_guardian.user_id`. `app.current_parent_user` **must be absent on staff sessions** and the parent policies apply only when set. (ii) a dedicated PG role = too big a portability change; (iii) app-layer only = what `public-receipt.ts` does but **fails Decision 13**, which mandates DB-layer enforcement. вҡ пёҸ `prod-paste-0055-parent-linkage.sql` must be hand-pasted or the boundary is silently app-layer-only.

### Lucy's additional findings (surface side)
- **The three real leak vectors are in the BUILD, not the mock** вҖ” the surface itself is clean (no rank/percentile/peer names; its notes forbid it twice): (1) **`wassce_papers` is COHORT-scoped** вҖ” driving В§2 from papers instead of `wassce_paper_sittings WHERE candidate_id` pulls other candidates' rows; (2) reusing any INCR-18/20 component, esp. `mock_results` teacher comments which contain literal cohort prose ("top quartile"); (3) `projection_snapshot_json.band` carries the cohort tier vocabulary. **"Omission isn't enforcement вҖ” a plain `tenant_isolation` policy lets a PARENT read every candidate in the school."**
- **рҹ”ҙ The drawn URL puts a child's NAME in the path** (`parent.omnischools.gh/asankrangwa/aidoo-yaa/wassce`) вҖ” the exact pattern this repo already forbids for boarding PII. **Resolve the child from the SESSION with no route parameter.**
- **Jargon gap:** `aggregate` is used 5Г— and **never defined** вҖ” FAQ Q5 explains why it hasn't moved but never what it IS or that LOWER IS BETTER, making "cut-off 11 В· one place inside" unreadable to a parent. Needs a ruling. The exemplary translation to copy: **`Missed В· medical` вҶ’ `Postponed В· SC-12 filed`** (needs a parent label map, not the shared staff constant). Must stay absent: predictor mock, moderation, best-3, tier band, credit pass, raw score.
- Existing precedent nobody had cited: **`lib/actions/public-receipt.ts`** вҖ” unguessable token + student code, unauthenticated, re-scoped downstream. The shipped "parent sees one child's artefact" pattern.

### Status
**Migration 0055 spec + full AC (L1-L6 linkage В· C1-C7 claiming В· D1-D10 crafted-request denials В· R1-R4 read scope В· A1-A2 ack-absence В· M1-M2 multi-school) are in Kofi's ruling.** Lucy map: `docs/senior/wassce-parent-surface-map.md`. **Blocked on the owner's claiming-flow call** (invite vs self-serve) before Wells is dispatched.

**OWNER DECISION (2026-07-20): claiming flow = school-issued INVITE.** Wells dispatched for 19a (migration 0055 + per-user RLS). Self-serve declined.

### INCR-19a В· Build + gate outcomes (PR #168 вҖ” awaiting owner merge)
- **Commits:** Wells schema/RLS `adc5ca1` + Claude Code claiming/deny-suite `cf57519` + Wells block-fix `90d006c`. Migration **0055** (`student_guardian.user_id` single-colвҶ’ref_user, `invite.student_id` compositeвҶ’students). Files: `db/schema/{students,invites}.ts`, `lib/db/rls.ts` (`withParentScope`), `db/sql/{policies.sql,prod-paste-0055-parent-linkage.sql}`, `lib/actions/invites.ts`, `lib/parent/{claim,parent-data}.ts` (+2 tests), `lib/access.ts` (`isStaff`), `components/students/parent-invite-button.tsx`, `scripts/verify-parent-boundary.ts`.
- **The per-user RLS boundary:** `app.current_parent_user` GUC + **RESTRICTIVE** `parent_deny` (deny-by-default) / `parent_scope` (9 readable tables via the `parent_student_ids` SECURITY DEFINER helper). RESTRICTIVE because `tenant_isolation` is permissive and Postgres OR's permissive policies вҖ” a permissive parent policy would leak the whole school. `pu IS NULL` no-op guard вҶ’ staff/bypass byte-unchanged. **`parent_deny` is CATALOG-DRIVEN** вҖ” every FORCE-RLS + `school_id` table lacking `parent_scope` is auto-denied, so a new tenant table inherits the boundary with zero code change (Dex's structural fix). A **drift-guard** in `verify-parent-boundary.ts` enumerates the same catalog and fails RED if any table is left unprotected.
- **TWO BLOCKS found + closed at their shared root cause (hand-maintained lists):** (1) **Sarah BLOCK вҖ” pre-existing health-PII exposure:** `student_health_record` (blood group/allergies/medications) was missing from `policies.sql` since 0036 вҶ’ **RLS OFF on dev** (a parent read every child's health record; unscoped read crossed tenants). **Prod was SAFE** вҖ” `prod-paste-0036` gave it `tenant_isolation`, owner-confirmed live (`rls_on`+`forced` both true). Fixed: added to `tenant_isolation` + auto-covered by the catalog deny. (2) **Dex BLOCK вҖ” `parent_deny` was a hand-kept 77-table array with no drift-guard** вҶ’ a new tenant table silently escaped. Fixed by the catalog-driven deny + drift-guard.
- **Gates ALL GREEN (re-gated after the fix):** Sarah **CLEAR-TO-MERGE** (leak proven closed as non-superuser role: parentвҶ’0 health rows, staffвҶ’own school; catalog complete 9 scope+78 deny, 0 both/neither; drift-guard bites вҖ” dropped a denyвҶ’REDвҶ’`db:policies`вҶ’GREEN). Dex **APPROVE** (set-algebra proof the catalog reproduces the exact prior 77+the health table; byte-identical policiesвҶ”prod-paste 170/170; scope-first ordering can't AND-lock a parent from their own child). Quinn **GREEN** (457 tests; deny suite proven NOT theatre вҖ” drops to `omnischools_app` rolsuper=f/rolbypassrls=f; every L1-6/C1-7/D1-10/M1-2 assertion holds). Deny suite = `db:verify-parent-boundary` (RLS can't run in pure vitest вҖ” MUST stay in the merge gate; NOT in `pnpm test`).
- **вҡ пёҸ PROD DEPLOY:** hand-paste `db/sql/prod-paste-0055-parent-linkage.sql` вҖ” installs the whole parent boundary + idempotently re-asserts the health-table `tenant_isolation`. Without it the boundary is app-layer only AND `student_health_record` has no `parent_deny` on prod (Sarah's exact leak, live).
- **NO parent write path** (Kofi R4, Lucy confirmed 0 write controls on the surface) вҖ” the signing UI is descoped to the senior backlog. `university_targets.parent_acknowledged_at` stays writerless.
- **рҹҹ  Deferred (non-blocking, logged):** (a) `REVOKE EXECUTE ON parent_student_ids FROM PUBLIC` + `GRANT TO omnischools_app` вҖ” low-sev RPC-surface hardening (the GRANT is MANDATORY or the rls-test/verify harness breaks with "permission denied for function"; the real app connects as owner so is unaffected). (b) Column redaction (`notes`/`filed_by_user_id`/`reg_flag`) is loader-discipline not structural вҖ” the 19b surface loader must keep selecting only parent-safe columns (a `select *` leaks); revisit a column-grant/DB-view when 19b lands. (c) `projection_snapshot_json.band` carries cohort-tier vocabulary вҖ” 19b MUST strip it before rendering (Lucy leak #3; dormant in 19a, no caller). (d) Minor test-coverage gaps (C3/C5/C4-overwrite verified by inspection, no automated assertion). (e) **Manual check for owner:** no browser tool here could click the staff "Invite to parent portal" button end-to-end вҖ” writes proven via the deny suite, a real click before ship is worth it.

### INCR-19b (NEXT вҖ” the read-only portal, no migration)
Own `app/(parent)/вҖҰ` route group (never admit PARENT into `app/(app)/`). В§1вҖ“В§5 minus the Sickbay-dependent content (omit ward/bed/clinician/NHIS/call-log вҖ” module 4.4 unbuilt, "omit not fake"). Resolve the child from the SESSION (no name/id in the URL вҖ” Lucy). ### INCR-19b В· Kofi parent-copy rulings + AC (2026-07-21) вҖ” read-only portal, NO migration
Proposed home: new `lib/wassce/parent-copy.ts` + a `PARENT_SITTING_LABEL` map beside the staff constant.
- **R1 aggregate defined (default; plan already directed it):** a FAQ item ("An aggregate totals a student's results вҖ” each grade is worth points, 1 for A1 up to 9 for F9, and the six subjects that count are added, so a LOWER aggregate is BETTER: 6 best, 54 lowest") + a В§1 gloss line under the target-meta ("A lower aggregate is better вҖ” Yaa's projected 10 is one point inside KNUST's cut-off of 11, so she is on course for her first choice"). Conveys best-6 WITHOUT exposing best-3 mechanics (excluded). Cut-off renders with its `(2025)` year, never bare.
- **R2 jargon map:** `PARENT_SITTING_LABEL` вҖ” satвҶ’"Sat В· attended"; exempted+open-SCвҶ’"Postponed В· SC-12 filed"; exempted+REJECTED-SCвҶ’"Not sat В· school to advise"; earliest futureвҶ’"Next paper В· {N} days"; other futureвҶ’"In {N} days"; null dateвҶ’"Upcoming" (NEVER "In NaN days"). NEVER render "Missed В· medical"/"Failed"/"Absent". SC-12 process steps + match-tier words (comfortable/stretch/safety) render bare (used AND explained). **Exclusion list (must never reach a parent):** moderat*, predictor(mock), best-3, tier-band/any `AGGREGATE_BANDS` label, cohort/rank/percentile/quartile/distribution/"N of 240", credit-pass, dropped-subject, raw-score, at-risk, `reg_flag`/`ON_MEDICAL`, SC `notes`/`filed_by_user_id`, superseded statements, `mock_results` teacher comments.
- **R3 signature HONESTY (ship now вҖ” honesty-corrective, not the owner-gated OTP flow):** PHONE_OTP вҶ’ "Acknowledgement recorded by the school В· confirmed by phone with +233вҖҰ on 28 March 2026." В· IN_PERSON/PDF_UPLOAD variants. **Must NOT contain "Phone-OTP signature" or an HH:MM GMT stamp** (minute precision is what reads as cryptographic). Card title "вҖҰacknowledged onвҖҰ" not "you signed on". `parent_acknowledged_at IS NULL` вҶ’ NO signature line, neutral "Not yet acknowledged вҖ” the school will contact you" note, **NO sign/OTP button** (would make it a write surface вҖ” R4). No statement row вҶ’ omit the card.
- **R3b DRAFT hidden** (loader already `ne(status,"DRAFT")`); parent-visible SC statuses = FILED/ACKNOWLEDGED/APPROVED/SCHEDULED/COMPLETED. **REJECTED not faked (safe degrade; рҹ”¶ OWNER-FLAG the deferral):** no 5-step/pulsing card, affected papers show "Not sat В· school to advise" (NOT "Postponed"), one calm line "вҖҰpapers need follow-up вҖ” {HoA} will call you." A fully-designed human-first REJECTED experience is deferred to the increment that ships the comms channel (freshness contract: the portal must not be where a parent first learns a hard fact).
- **R4 multi-school notice:** when `hasChildrenAtOtherSchools===true`, top-of-portal banner "You have children registered at more than one school. This portal is showing {activeSchool} only. To see a child at another school, contact that school's office." (children at the SAME school = a header switcher, separate/L.2.)

# MODULE 4.4 вҖ” SICKBAY (5 surfaces В· size L В· INCR-21 вҶ’ INCR-28) вҖ” Pence plan 2026-07-21
**Constitution:** `md files/BUILD_STACK.md` L343вҖ“371 (8 enums + 14 tables) + L584вҖ“612 (the 12 decisions) вҖ” as 4.3 built to its BUILD_STACK batch. **Lucy inventory:** `docs/senior/sickbay-surface-inventory.md` (30 NEEDS-SCHEMA shapes N1вҖ“N30, 14 NO-BINDING B1вҖ“B14, 24 NHIS elements, 6 medical-PII classes, 15 fabricated demo items, 20 open questions).
**Surfaces:** `sickbay-setup` В· `sickbay-today` В· `sickbay-visit-record` В· `sickbay-chronic-register` В· `sickbay-referral-log`.

### Reconciliations (recorded)
- Board said "(4) size M" вҶ’ **5 surfaces, size L**. The missed one is `sickbay-setup` вҖ” the config spine every other surface reads, so the estimate was short a whole config table set.
- вң… **`fix/migrate-0033-fk-ordering` is STALE/CLOSED, NOT an orphan.** The `-main` variant `bba67ee` merged via **PR #149**; `db/migrations/0033_flowery_vector.sql` on main has every `*_tenant_uk` UNIQUE (L67+) ahead of every composite FK (L153+). Verified by reading the file, not branch topology (the isolated worktree still sits checked out on the superseded branch, which is what makes it *look* unmerged). **Nothing to fold in.** Residual risk is the different, real one: no CI replays the migrate chain (OWNER-TODO #14) and 0044вҶ’0055 added ~35 composite FKs since вҖ” INCR-21 runs one from-empty `db:migrate` as a gate step.
- `MATRON` already exists in `appRoleEnum`/`KnownAppRole` (reserved sickbay-only since INCR-7) and `boarding_bunk.prefect_role` already carries `'SICKBAY'` (Sick Bay Prefect, display-only). **No new RBAC role** вҖ” `SICKBAY_ROLES = [ADMIN, HEADMASTER, MATRON]` for module access (clinical READ is narrower вҖ” see D2).

### рҹ”ҙ OWNER DECISIONS вҖ” ANSWERED 2026-07-21
- **D1 В· Clinical narrative вҶ’ STORE IT.** Owner consciously accepts holding special-category health data (Ghana DPA 2012): working impressions, red-flag screens, named diagnoses incl. mental health. Owner confirms the school's lawful basis / parental-consent path. вҡ пёҸ The surfaces deliberately say `working_impression`, NOT `diagnosis` вҖ” a scope-of-practice commitment (Lucy). **Preserve that vocabulary verbatim.**
- **D2 В· Clinical read default вҶ’ MATRON + HEADMASTER by default; ADMIN grant-only.** (Owner chose the middle option over blanket grant-only.) вҡ пёҸ The surface's "admin-private" means *school leadership*, NOT this codebase's `ADMIN` (proprietor/IT). ADMIN gets module access but **no clinical read without an explicit, expiring, per-student grant**. HMs per-grant (derive candidacy from `house.hm_user_id`, don't store it). **OPEN sub-ruling for INCR-23 (Kofi):** Lucy classes mental health as a distinct special category (bereavement, psychiatric dx, self-harm escalation) вҖ” does the HEADMASTER default extend to it, or does that tier stay grant-only too? Not needed before INCR-23.
- **D3 В· NHIS вҶ’ IN.** Owner accepts storing the national identifier. вҡ пёҸ **My question framed it as "2 columns on `student_health_record`" вҖ” Lucy's read shows that is too simple and the answer's SHAPE is unsettled.** The surfaces need 4 shapes: card identity; **card-holder вү  student** (referral log В§02 renders `NHIS-9842-1276-5503 В· A. Aidoo В· Yaa Aidoo (minor)` вҖ” the card is the *mother's*, arguing household/guardian not student); per-line-item coverage on referral costs; `accepts_nhis` on hospital config. The direction (store it) STANDS; **the modelling is a Kofi+Wells ruling at INCR-25** вҖ” not blocking INCR-21/22. рҹҡ« The school-wide card-health roll-up (`1,108 / 1,200 В· 92.3% В· "Synced from student records"`) is **this module's STPSHS matrix вҖ” DO NOT BUILD IT.**
- **D4 В· Attendance-M вҶ’ sickbay writes `MEDICAL`; a teacher save CANNOT downgrade it.** `reasonCode='SICKBAY'`; correction only via the existing co-signed `attendance_correction` flow. **Root-cause guard in the ONE shared writer** (`lib/actions/attendance.ts` `saveAttendance` `onConflictDoUpdate`), never per-caller. Sickbay WRITES attendance (rejected: attendance derives from sickbay вҖ” would push the derivation into ~8 shipped Basic-tier consumers).
