**Recommend MOVING to backlog:** F3 discipline-pause / WASSCE-window absence exemption (Decision 6) is **boarding Г— WASSCE with NO sickbay dependency** вҖ” parked here by association only. Kofi call.

### Risks
1. **рҹ”ҙ Third RLS boundary (INCR-23).** D2's per-staff grants must be DB-enforced (BUILD_STACK Decision 5: *"RLS on Postgres enforces this; the application layer cannot bypass it"*) вҶ’ a `staff_grant_scope` RESTRICTIVE family on a new `app.current_staff_user` GUC mirroring the shipped 19a `parent_scope`/`parent_deny` (`db/sql/policies.sql:258вҖ“451`) + a verifier cloned from `scripts/verify-parent-boundary.ts`. The single most novel item in 4.4. App-layer-only grants contradict the constitution AND the surface copy вҖ” do not take that shortcut without a Kofi override.
   вң… **Good news:** `parent_deny` is catalog-driven, so **every new sickbay table is parent-denied with zero edits** вҖ” the correct default for all of them (D8).
2. **рҹ”ҙ The attendance-M path loses data if built naively.** (a) `uniq_attendance_student_day` + `onConflictDoUpdate` overwrite вҶ’ a matron's 09:14 MEDICAL is silently replaced by a teacher's 10:00 save (D4 guard fixes at the root). (b) `saveAttendance` refuses writes into a CLOSED term вҖ” the sickbay writer must respect that too. (c) **`attendance_record.class_id` is NOT NULL**, and the 240 synthetic F3 WASSCE candidates (`db/seed/wassce.ts:222`) have **no `classId`/house/residency** вҖ” so **Y. Aidoo, the canonical cross-module demo case, cannot receive an attendance row at all** and can never appear in the boarding sick-bay count. Fix the seed or honestly skip classless students вҖ” **decide before INCR-22, not during INCR-28's demo.**
   (d) Lucy B-item: the surface's **`5 periods В· all classes` is impossible** вҖ” `uniq_attendance_student_day` means per-period attendance does not exist. Omit or re-express as a day mark.
3. **рҹҹ  "Every read is audited" is a volume/perf trap.** `lib/db/audit.ts` logs mutations only, but 8 of the 11 audit rows on the register are View/Export. Naive per-read logging = write amplification on a hot path + an audit table outgrowing the data. Recommend: audit **care-plan detail opens only**, never the list view, deduped one row per (actor Г— student Г— day). Kofi/Dex.
4. **рҹҹ  Medical PII leaks by PROXIMITY, not just by field** (Lucy, sharp): the bed tile prints `SCD` beside a name; the setup stock row reads `Hydroxyurea 500mg В· for Adwoa Mensa` вҖ” **a diagnosis leaking through an inventory table**. Sarah must gate adjacency, not just column lists. The deliberate non-disclosure copy (*"medical detail withheld"*, *"'M' not 'A'"*, *"Diagnosis stays inside the sickbay module"*) **is the product вҖ” preserve verbatim.**
5. **рҹҹ  Boarding in-House conflict (NEW, Lucy):** OQ5 ruled sick-bay is NOT subtracted from in-House (sickbay is on-site) вҖ” but a **referred-out** student genuinely IS off-campus. Sickbay-admitted вү  referred-out. Kofi must split the two before INCR-28.
6. **рҹҹ  5 prod-pastes of the most sensitive data yet.** A missed paste leaks medical PII across schools. Sarah gates paste parity per increment; module close re-runs `db/sql/verify-prod-rls.sql`.
7. **рҹҹЎ Mode C is ~half the market.** ~49% of public SHS have no sickbay. `REFERRAL_ONLY` must be first-class from INCR-21 (referrals + chronic + notifications, no beds/rounds/admissions) вҖ” empty-by-design, not broken. Quinn AC at 21, not discovered at 25.
8. **рҹҹЎ Scope ceilings (Decision 12):** 24 stock items + reorder points, nothing more. Not a pharmacy, not an EMR. Vitals timeline is a log, not a monitor. No diagnosis vocabulary beyond `chronic_condition_enum`.
9. **рҹҹЎ Seed drift blocks the demo (Lucy: 15 fabricated items).** Surfaces name **Kufuor/Nkrumah** Houses (seeded: AggreyВ·GuggisbergВ·FraserВ·SlessorВ·KingsleyВ·Aryee); **Adwoa Mensa** (the SCD anchor on 4 of 5 surfaces) doesn't exist (seed has *Abena Mensah*); **two Aidoos** вҖ” `ASK-23-0007 Yaw` (MALE, DAY) vs `SHS-2023-0817 Yaa` (FEMALE, ON_MEDICAL); the referral log prints `SHS-2023-0817`, so the sickbay case is the **WASSCE** Aidoo. Also **4 different Slessor housemasters**, 4 student-code formats, **3 contradictory round schedules** (which proves rounds must be config-driven). Kofi/Lucy to settle before INCR-28.
10. **рҹҹЎ `student_health_record.studentId` carries a GLOBAL `.unique()`** (`db/schema/students.ts:250`) not the tenant-scoped idiom вҖ” harmless with UUIDs, but it is *why* chronic conditions need their own table (one health record per student; a student can carry two chronic conditions). Wells note.

### INCR-21 В· Kofi rulings + AC (2026-07-21) В· Lucy map: `docs/senior/sickbay-setup-surface-map.md` вҖ” F0 spine, migration **0056**
**Scope:** `sickbay-setup` В§1 (mode В· clinical staff В· health prefects) + В§2 (beds В· hours/rounds) + В§5 policy anchors (static). В§3 stockвҶ’INCR-24, В§4 hospitalsвҶ’INCR-25 вҖ” **absent entirely, no shell/badge/anchor target.** NO visits, NO patients, NO clinical PII beyond the matron's N&MC number. **No split** (smaller than INCR-8 which shipped whole); splitting would cost a 2nd prod paste of the same table family.
- **R1 naming** вҖ” module-wide singular `sickbay_*`: `sickbay_settings`/`sickbay_bed`/`sickbay_schedule_slot` (repo idiom over BUILD_STACK's mixed plurals; unprefixed `referrals`/`drug_stock` would collide with billing/pharmacy).
- **R2 one sickbay per school** вҖ” `sickbay_settings.school_id NOT NULL UNIQUE` (the `boarding_settings` singleton idiom); **NO child carries `sickbay_id`** (it would be a derived duplicate of `school_id` + a 2nd composite FK on every table; no boarding table carries a `boarding_settings_id`).
- **R3/R4 mode is an AFFORDANCE filter, never a data filter** вҖ” one schema, all three modes, no row deleted/hidden/migrated on switch (BUILD_STACK L588 verbatim). **A and B are capability-IDENTICAL** (differ in editorial copy only вҖ” do NOT gate anything on A-vs-B in 4.4). **C (REFERRAL_ONLY) disables:** beds, isolation, admissions, schedule slots, medication rounds, visiting doctor, standing orders, drug stock. **C KEEPS:** visit record (disposition REFER/DISCHARGE, never ADMIT), chronic register, referrals, parent notifications, health prefects, policy anchors.
- **R5 Mode C renders empty-by-design with the reason NAMED** вҖ” В§2 absent from the DOM entirely; ONE explanatory panel (no on-site beds/rounds; prefects are first response; cases route to referral hospitals). **Never `0/0`, never `вҖ”`, never a disabled control, never a PLACEHOLDER badge.** В§1 promotes the prefect card ABOVE clinical staff (in C the prefects ARE the front line). Risk 7 discharged at 21, not discovered at 25.
- **R6 mode changes are lossless + reversible** вҖ” BвҶ’C retains every bed/slot row (unread, not deleted); CвҶ’B returns identical bed numbers. **No `frozen_at`** вҖ” a sickbay is live operational config (do NOT copy the WASSCE freeze). Guard landing at 22: reject вҶ’REFERRAL_ONLY while an admission is open.
- **R7 bed-as-a-row, own table, NOT `boarding_bunk`** вҖ” 3 independent reasons: bunks are dormitory/House-scoped (a sickbay bed has no House); `students.current_bunk_id` is one-per-student but a patient occupies her dorm bunk AND a sickbay bed simultaneously (reuse would vacate her dorm bunk and silently corrupt the boarding in-House count); sickbay occupancy is hours-scale and belongs to an admission.
- **R8 `bed_number smallint`, `UNIQUE(school_id,bed_number)`, STABLE FOR LIFE** вҖ” retiring bed 4 never renumbers 5вҶ’4 (a visit record saying "bed 3" must still mean that bed); next = `max+1`. **R9 `is_isolation` boolean; the two pools NEVER merge** (surface: *"The two numbers can't pool"*) вҖ” a full general pool does not overflow into isolation.
- **R10 bed counts DERIVED from rows вҖ” NO `capacity_beds`/`isolation_beds` scalars** (BUILD_STACK carries both models; a stored count that can disagree with the rows is the STPSHS-matrix failure in miniature). **R11 capacity edit = target reconcile, never delete** вҖ” decrease deactivates highest-numbered UNOCCUPIED beds; if unreachable without deactivating an occupied bed the WHOLE save is rejected, named error, no partial application.
- **R13 canonical slot set = setup В§02's 7 rows VERBATIM** вҖ” the setup surface IS the config spine, so `today`'s 17:00 round and the chronic register's 13:00 column are demo drift and LOSE. **The canonical medication rounds are THREE: 06:30 / 12:30 / 21:00** (INCR-24 fires off exactly these; the 4th is dropped, not seeded). Descriptions are STORED (*"when the matron is on leave the description is the handoff document"*).
- **R14 day applicability = `days_of_week` ISO set + `runs_on_holidays` вҖ” REJECT reusing `boardingDayTypeEnum`** (it answers "what rhythm is today", not "which days does this slot run", and literally cannot express `Thursdays` or `Every day В· 365` вҖ” forcing it would silently drop the visiting doctor's weekday). One pure formatter reproduces all 5 surface labels; **never store the label beside the set.**
- **R15 `sickbay_slot_kind` enum** (`MEDICATION_ROUND|CLINIC|DOCTOR_VISIT|ON_CALL`) вҖ” else INCR-24 must string-match labels to find rounds.
- **R16 anchor semantics** вҖ” exactly ONE per school (partial unique index, the `uniq_mock_exam_predictor` idiom); kind MUST be MEDICATION_ROUND; **time IS editable** (05:45 is still anchored); cannot be deleted/deactivated/re-kinded/un-anchored and none can be promoted; **must be вүӨ every other medication round's start** (else "morning round" sorts after evening and INCR-24's ordering is nonsense). A/B must have one; C has none.
- **R17 NO `operating_hours_json`/`visiting_doctor_schedule_json`** вҖ” both describe facts the slot rows already hold relationally; two mechanisms for one fact is exactly how the 3 contradictory schedules got into the surfaces.
- **R18/R19 authz вҖ” `SICKBAY_ROLES=[ADMIN,HEADMASTER,MATRON]` (read), `SICKBAY_CONFIG_WRITE_ROLES=[ADMIN,HEADMASTER]` (write В§1/В§2).** **The MATRON READS but CANNOT WRITE В§1/В§2** вҖ” not mode, not beds, not schedule (she must see her own hours + bed inventory). В§3 flips to `[ADMIN,MATRON]` at INCR-24. Grounding: the surface's sidebar footer is the Headmaster on В§1/В§2/В§4/В§5 and switches to the Matron on В§3 alone вҖ” *intentional and load-bearing*. HOUSEMASTER is NOT a member (HM reach is grant-scoped at INCR-23, never role-scoped). Footer renders the ACTING user, never a hardcoded name.
- **R20 Assistant Matron / School Nurse = the same `MATRON` role**, distinguished only by which pointer holds them (`matron_user_id`вҶ’"Senior Matron", `assistant_matron_user_id`вҶ’"Assistant Matron"). No seniority column, no `sickbay_staff` table, no new role. Both nullable; both must hold MATRON in that school вҖ” validated at the APP layer, never a cross-table DB trigger (the boarding "Kofi trap J3" precedent).
- **R21 the visiting doctor is NOT a system user** вҖ” `visiting_doctor_name`/`_affiliation` text + the DOCTOR_VISIT slot. No `ref_user`, no `role_assignment`, no invite, no login. An account for a 3-hour-a-week external clinician creates a tenant identity, a password, an audit actor and a leaving problem, for a name on a card. His clinical artefacts are attributed at 22/23 as *recorded external actors* (name+affiliation stamped, authored by the transcribing matron).
- **R22 N&MC = 2 columns on `staff_profile`** beside the shipped `ntc_licence_*` вҖ” **reject the generalised `licence_body` refactor**: a teacher-turned-matron holds BOTH licences and one generalised triple cannot hold two. Sarah note: an N&MC number is a **public statutory-register credential, NOT medical PII**; it is the only new "clinical" datum in 0056.
- **R23 health-prefect roster = DERIVED READ of `boarding_bunk.prefect_role='SICKBAY'`** вҖ” **reject BUILD_STACK's `school_health_prefect_student_ids JSONB`: an id array is un-FK-able, so it cannot carry the composite `(school_id,id)` tenant FK the schema rests on вҶ’ a foreign-school student id could be written in with nothing to stop it. A tenant-isolation hole for a display list.** 6 marked bunks (one per House) yields the surface's *"6 students В· covers all 6 houses"* with real referential integrity + zero new storage. **OMIT** seniority/training-date/rotation (no backing). Zero marked bunks вҶ’ honest empty state pointing at Boarding. вҡ пёҸ **Supersedes Lucy N30b** (she proposed a roster table); Kofi rules derive-now, and escalates the day-student gap as E3.
- **R24 frozen contract `lib/sickbay/{config,defaults}.ts`** in the `getExeatPolicy`/`getScheduleTemplate` idiom вҖ” server-only reader + pure DB-free unit-tested defaults. `getSickbayConfig` / `getScheduleSlots` / `getRoundSchedule(вҶ’MEDICATION_ROUND subset, anchor first)`. **FROZEN:** every type/field name, the 3 getter signatures, both enum value sets, `bedNumber` as bed identity, R16's anchor semantics. **LIVE:** mode, staff pointers, doctor, bed rows, slot times/labels/days/staffing. `capabilities` is DERIVED from mode by a pure function вҖ” **never stored, never hand-set.**
- **R25 a missing config row coalesces to `REFERRAL_ONLY` + `configured:false`** вҖ” never null, never fabricating capacity. Defaulting to FULL-with-8-beds would assert clinical capacity a school never declared; REFERRAL_ONLY is both the safe default and the statistical one (~49%).
- **R26 policy anchors are FROZEN CONSTANTS, not `notes_json`** вҖ” identical static editorial for every school; a per-school free-text JSON column invites per-tenant drift in a regulatory citation (LI 683, 1971).
- **R27 OMIT (no placeholder, no zero, no stub):** `Currently occupied 1/8 В· Adwoa Mensa В· bed 3 В· since 09:14` вҶ’ **omit the whole tile** (no admission table exists; even `0/8` is a hardcoded assertion about an entity the system cannot see) В· `Avg. weekly load 2.4` вҶ’ omit (needs a semester of history; `0.0` asserts a *measured* zero) В· staff status pills `On shift`/`Off В· back 18:00` вҶ’ omit (no shift roster), render a static role pill instead В· `11 years here` вҶ’ omit В· prefect seniority/training/rotation вҶ’ omit В· В§3/В§4/the 3-tier notification table/`Save & acknowledge` вҶ’ **absent entirely** В· sub-nav shows **only `Setup`** (omit-not-fake applies to navigation). вҡ пёҸ Doctor pill `Tomorrow` MAY render (derivable from the DOCTOR_VISIT `daysOfWeek`).
- **R28 the mode percentages (~16/~30/~59%) ship VERBATIM as static copy** вҖ” they do NOT sum to 105%: the third is a % of the ~49% *without* a sickbay, a different denominator (matches BUILD_STACK L588). Never computed, never stored.
- **Forward rulings:** **R29** sickbay-admitted вү  referred-out вҖ” OQ5's "sick-bay NOT subtracted from in-House" STANDS (on-site) and its gloss stays; a **referred-out** student IS subtracted, same bucket as an exeat. Two states, two treatments (binds 25/28). **R30** `5 periods В· all classes` вҶ’ re-express as a single day mark (`uniq_attendance_student_day`; don't escalate to per-period attendance for a copy string) (binds 22). **R31** F3 discipline-pause/WASSCE-window exemption вҶ’ **move to backlog** (boarding Г— WASSCE, no sickbay dependency) вҖ” confirmed.
**AC (Quinn) A1вҖ“A8 В· B1вҖ“B7 В· C1вҖ“C9 В· D1вҖ“D7 В· E1вҖ“E6 В· F1вҖ“F6 В· G1вҖ“G3.** Highlights: A2 (FULLвүЎFIRST_AID capabilities) В· A5 (no row вҶ’ REFERRAL_ONLY/configured:false, no throw, no null) В· A6 (BвҶ’CвҶ’B returns identical rows) В· A7 (Mode C: В§2 absent from DOM, no 0/вҖ”/disabled/placeholder) В· B4 (retire bed 4 вҶ’ next is 9) В· B6 (`sickbay_bed_tenant_uk` authored in 0056 though nothing references it until 0057) В· C3 (2nd anchor fails the partial unique) В· C5 (anchor time editable, but rejected if later than another round) В· C7 (`Thursdays` вҖ” a value `boarding_day_type` cannot express, proving non-reuse) В· C8 (22:00вҶ’06:00 midnight wrap ACCEPTED) В· D4 (doctor has NO ref_user/role_assignment/invite) В· D7 (zero marked bunks вҶ’ honest empty, not a count of 6) В· E2/E3 (MATRON read-only incl. direct POST) В· E5 (FORCE+tenant_isolation+auto parent_deny, verify don't assume) В· F2 (the omit-strings appear NOWHERE in the rendered surface) В· G1 (**from-empty `db:migrate` replay is a manual gate step** вҖ” no CI does it) В· G2 (0056 = exactly 2 enums + 3 tables + 2 columns, nothing clinical).
**рҹ”¶ OWNER-ESCALATE:** **E1** Mode-C staff-card title (no surface renders Mode C) вҖ” recommend `School Health Coordinator В· SHEP`, same `matron_user_id` pointer + MATRON role; **non-blocking, defaults to the recommendation.** **E2** six BUILD_STACK amendments (see below). **E3** the R23 derivation means a **DAY STUDENT cannot be a health prefect** вҖ” fine for Asankrangwa (720 boarders/480 day) and the boarding-prefect tradition, but possibly wrong for a **day-heavy Mode-C school, which is exactly where prefects ARE the entire clinical front line.** Recommend ship the derivation now; if day students must be eligible that is a small `sickbay_health_prefect` table at a later increment, NOT a change to 0056.
### INCR-21 В· Build + gate outcomes (PR #172 вҖ” awaiting owner merge) вҖ” вҡ пёҸ prod deploy: hand-paste `prod-paste-0056-sickbay-spine.sql`
- **Commits:** Wells schema/migration/RLS `a4e7e90` В· Claude Code impl `b7796cd` В· gate rework `138fb4a` В· Dex D1/D2 `a67db6e`. Migration **0056** = exactly 2 enums + 3 tables + 2 columns (AC G2). Files: `db/schema/sickbay.ts`, `db/sql/{policies.sql,prod-paste-0056-sickbay-spine.sql}`, `lib/sickbay/{defaults.ts(+test),config.ts}`, `lib/actions/sickbay-config.ts`, `db/seed/sickbay.ts`, `app/(app)/senior/sickbay/setup/page.tsx`, `components/sickbay/setup-console.tsx`, `lib/access.ts`, `scripts/rls-test.ts`.
- **Gates ALL GREEN:** Quinn **GREEN (sustained)** вҖ” AC A1вҖ“G3; **14 mutants run, all killed** after the rework; anchor ordering proven closed on **four** distinct paths through real server actions; A6 losslessness proven live *including a Mode-C staff save*; copy compared **character-exact** (`===`, not regex) against the surface HTML; 536 tests. Dex **APPROVE** вҖ” frozen contract matches R24, client/server seam **STRUCTURAL** (`defaults.ts` is import-free so it cannot regress into a data module; `config.ts` is `server-only`), portability clean (no trigger, no vendor primitive), D2 truth table walked across all 3 branches. Sarah **CLEAR-TO-MERGE** вҖ” attacker probe run as the **non-superuser `omnischools_app` role**: unset GUC / forged school id / claimed-parent session / cross-tenant INSERT / **row-relocation `UPDATE ... SET school_id=<foreign>`** all rejected (the `WITH CHECK` means a school cannot *export* a row either); `authorizeWrite()` is the first statement of all 6 mutations; no IDOR (slot ids re-resolved server-side + explicit predicate + RLS = 3 layers; bed ids never client-supplied); no new dep, no secret, no `sql.raw`.
- **рҹ”ҙ 3 gate BLOCKERS found + closed (`138fb4a`):** (1) **a Mode-C school could NEVER finish setup** вҖ” save enabled only on a mode *change*, but a fresh school already coalesces to `REFERRAL_ONLY` вҶ’ button permanently disabled, `configuredAt` never written, `configured:false` forever for **~49% of the market**, while the page rendered "Mode C В· selected" with a gold dot on a school that declared *nothing* (inverting the exact distinction R25 created `configured` to preserve). Found **independently by both gates** (Dex REQUIRED-B == Quinn MINOR-2). (2) **anchor-ordering enforced on 1 path of 4** вҖ” R16 states a property of the SET but the check fired only when the edited slot WAS the anchor; a non-anchor round could be moved earlier, or the anchor moved past an *inactive* round which was then toggled on (Quinn found a 4th: *edit* a parked round earlier while off, then toggle on). Replaced by one pure set-level `validateRoundOrdering(slotsAfterChange)` called from **both** writers. (3) **`getRoundSchedule` returned INACTIVE rounds** вҖ” a round the headmaster switched off would still fire at INCR-24; fixed now because changing a frozen getter's semantics later is a cross-increment break.
- **рҹ”ҙ Dex D1/D2 (2nd round) вҶ’ FIXED (`a67db6e`):** **D1** the doctor fields' absent-means-unchanged semantic was half-applied вҖ” `matronUserId`/`assistantMatronUserId` still treated absence as CLEAR while the schema declared all four `.nullish()`, so a POST of just `{visitingDoctorName}` would wipe both matron pointers (unreachable from today's UI, but the first partial editor added in 22вҖ“28 hits it). Both moved to `.nullable()` вҶ’ absence **rejected at the trust boundary**. **D2** the audit `after` had become a *patch* while `before` stayed a *snapshot*, so an auditor could not distinguish "doctor unchanged" from "doctor cleared" вҖ” live on every Mode-C staff save. DB write stays a patch; `recordAudit` now gets the effective snapshot (AC E4 restored).
- **рҹҹў Tooling fix (Quinn):** `db:rls-test` used **exact** seeded counts, so every legitimate seed addition (INCR-21's 2 MATRON assignments) turned it permanently RED вҖ” at which point a real isolation regression hides among standing failures. Now `MIN_OWN_ROWS`/`assertAtLeast` (a **liveness floor**); the two directions that actually prove isolation (foreign school id, unset GUC) stay **exact-zero**. Proven to still go RED by widening `tenant_isolation` to `USING(true)` on `sickbay_bed`, then restored.
- **Honest omissions (omit-not-fake):** `Currently occupied` + `Avg. weekly load` tiles omitted **entirely** вҖ” no admission/visit table exists, so even `0 / 8` asserts something about an entity the system cannot see (a *false zero*, distinct from a known-zero). Staff shift pills, `11 years here`, prefect seniority/training/rotation omitted (no backing). В§3/В§4/the 3-tier notification table absent entirely вҖ” no shell, no badge, no anchor target. Sub-nav shows only `Setup`.
- **рҹҹ  INCR-24 obligations (recorded, deliberately NOT fixed вҖ” they only bite once 0059's medication tables carry `(school_id, slot_id)`):** (a) **`resetScheduleSlots` is a hard DELETE** that changes every slot id вҶ’ must become a reconcile/update-in-place, or a "Reset to defaults" cascades away medication-administration rows against the append-only MAR rule. (b) **`validateRoundOrdering` TOCTOU** вҖ” the slot set is read *outside* the write tx (`sickbay-config.ts:307,365`), so two concurrent admins can both validate against pre-change state and commit a violating set; fix is a `FOR UPDATE` read inside `withSchool`. (c) a future **slot-create** action must refuse a second anchor (`validateRoundOrdering` takes `rounds.find(isAnchor)`; the partial unique index is the only guard today). (d) the B5 reject branch stays unit-test-only until INCR-22 supplies real `occupiedBedIds` вҖ” grep `planBedReconcile(config.beds, parsed.data, [])`.
- **рҹҹ  Sarah advisories for INCR-22вҖ“28 (none block 21):** (1) **the data-minimisation argument EXPIRES at INCR-23** вҖ” today every reader holds `SICKBAY_ROLES` so prop-trimming is hygiene, but 23 introduces grant-scoped HOUSEMASTER reach into health data and "the reader is privileged anyway" becomes false; make the Mode-C gating pattern (`page.tsx:78-88`) the rule before the first clinical prop crosses. (2) **`holdsMatronRole` is the ONLY tenancy guard on the matron pointers** вҖ” `ref_user` is global so the DB cannot stop a foreign user id; every future clinical actor pointer (attending clinician, prescriber) needs the same explicit app-layer check, and where the target is a *tenant* row use a composite `(school_id,id)` FK instead. (3) `days_of_week` has no DB CHECK вҖ” fine while `updateScheduleSlot` is the only writer; a bulk import/template-apply path must route through `SlotSchema` or add a CHECK. (4) `AUTH_DEV_BYPASS` must stay false in prod or the audit actor on the product's most sensitive module is untrustworthy. (5) `getHealthPrefects` returns raw student UUIDs as React keys вҖ” harmless now, a cross-reference handle if that component is reused under a lower read gate.
- **рҹҹЎ Non-blocking:** `configuredAt` is overwritten on every mode save, so the column no longer answers "first configured when" (`configured` boolean is unaffected) вҖ” use `coalesce(configured_at, now())` if the first-time answer matters. `validateRoundOrdering` compares times ignoring `daysOfWeek` (a Sunday-only 05:00 round is rejected against a weekday 06:30 anchor) вҖ” conservative and consistent with `roundSchedule`'s global ordering; INCR-24 may want per-day. Mode-C `form` staleness is prevented only by an *accidental* remount (the card-order swap changes React's index-based reconciliation) вҖ” if someone keys those children or drops the swap, a CвҶ’B switch could render an empty doctor input over a stored doctor (non-destructive by construction since absent вү  cleared, but the protection is incidental).
- **Quinn's ruling on the compensating control:** no DOM test stack. The save rule is a pure `canSaveMode()` with 5 asserted cases; selection state / gold dot / payload contents were proven from the **served HTML + flight payload** (the real build serving real props вҖ” better than jsdom); the residual gap is 3 non-branching wiring lines whose failure mode is now a *no-op* rather than data loss. **Condition to revisit:** the first client component in this module holding state that can diverge from its server props and be written back (optimistic update, multi-step wizard).

## INCR-21 вң… MERGED (PR #172, `a4e7e90`+`b7796cd`+`138fb4a`+`a67db6e`) вҖ” Sickbay F0 spine В· migration 0056 В· вҡ пёҸ prod-paste `prod-paste-0056-sickbay-spine.sql` RUN by owner 2026-07-21

### INCR-22 В· Kofi rulings R32вҖ“R67 + AC (2026-07-21) В· Lucy map: `docs/senior/sickbay-visit-surface-map.md` вҖ” THE TRUNK, size XL, **SPLITS 22a/22b/22c**, migration **0057**
**Scope:** `visit-record` В§01 (identity + vitals timeline) В§02 (assessment + consult) В§04 (disposition + criteria) + `today` В§01 (queue + bed board). Tables: `sickbay_visit`, `sickbay_vital_reading`, `sickbay_admission`, `sickbay_doctor_consult`.

**рҹ”ҙ R67 SPLIT вҖ” three gated slices, ONE milestone branch, ONE migration, ONE prod paste** (the seam is where no migration crosses, so it costs the owner zero extra hand-pastes вҖ” the objection that kept INCR-21 whole does not apply):
| Slice | Contents | Migration |
|---|---|---|
| **22a** | 0057 (2 enums + 4 tables) + RLS/policies/prod-paste, `lib/sickbay/{visits,vitals}.ts`, the visit write path (createВ·beginВ·assessВ·disposeВ·admitВ·dischargeВ·voidВ·consult), visit-record В§01/В§02/В§04, R56 mode guard, R59 real `occupiedBedIds` | **0057** |
| **22b** | `lib/attendance/mark.ts` extraction + the D4 guard + the **R49b SMS/audit fix**, `lib/sickbay/medical-hold.ts`, push+pull, R50 label, R51 correction fix, the R53 seed fix, the В§04 attendance line | none |
| **22c** | `today` В§01 (live strip, admitted block, queue, bed board) вҖ” pure derived reads. **+ today В§03 "Recent visits В· 24h"** (Lucy's boundary gap: assigned to NO increment on the board yet it is the ONLY route into a visit record; needs only 0057) | none |
рҹ”ҙ **22a and 22b MUST reach main TOGETHER.** 22a alone ships an admission that does not excuse attendance вҖ” a student in a bed gets marked ABSENT by her teacher and her mother gets an SMS saying so. That interim state must never exist in production. 22c may merge separately. 22b/22c branch **independently off the milestone head, never stacked** (orphan-PR rule).

**A В· lifecycle:** **R32** NO status column вҖ” state derived from 4 timestamps (`presented_at`/`started_at`/`disposition`+`disposition_at`/`voided_at` + the admission's `discharged_at`) via a pure `visitState()` in `lib/sickbay/visits.ts`; a stored enum can disagree with its own timestamps (R10 again). **R33** queue = not voided, not started, no disposition, presented today; the wait clock stops at **Begin visit**, not at assessment. **R34** disposition preconditions: `started_at` set В· complaint non-empty В· attending holds MATRON (`holdsMatronRole` reused) В· **`working_impression` required for ADMIT and REFER only** вҖ” a routine discharge is Tier-1 non-event and forcing prose on a 40-second dressing change produces garbage, not a record. **R35** ADMIT + admission row are ONE transaction. **R36** disposition IMMUTABLE at 22 (ADMITвҶ’REFER escalation вҶ’ INCR-25 as a referral *event*, never a mutation). **R37** nothing hard-deleted; a visit is VOIDABLE **only while open** (`disposition IS NULL`) вҖ” an open visit on the wrong student is an *active attendance-coercion source*. **R38** recorded external actors (Sick Bay Prefect at intake, visiting doctor) are **TEXT, never identity pointers** вҖ” an FK to the prefect student would place one student's identity as an *actor* inside another student's clinical record.
**B В· authz:** **R39** clinical WRITE = `[MATRON]` only (not ADMIN, not HEADMASTER вҖ” he reads but must never author an impression). **R40** clinical READ at 22 = **`SICKBAY_CLINICAL_READ_ROLES = [HEADMASTER, MATRON]`; ADMIN keeps module access and gets NO clinical detail** вҖ” INCR-23 EXTENDS this gate (`role вҲҲ READ || hasGrant(actor, student)`) rather than replacing it. вҡ пёҸ **Lucy Q2 independently found the same thing and rates it build-blocking:** reusing the shipped `SICKBAY_ROLES` (which includes ADMIN) as the read gate hands the proprietor/IT account every impression, vital and complaint вҖ” contradicting owner D2. ADMIN's props must be **server-side trimmed**, not conditionally rendered (Sarah INCR-21 advisory 1 lands here). **R41** the HOUSEMASTER boundary is a **field-limited FUNCTION SIGNATURE**, not a grant, and lives at INCR-28: a separate reader returning `{studentId, studentName, admittedAt}` вҖ” structurally incapable of returning a complaint. Do NOT build a general `getAdmissions()` that 28 can reuse. **R42** D2 sub-ruling ANSWERED: the acute visit record is NOT tiered at 22 (mental-health content is unclassifiable free text); at **23** the HEADMASTER default does **NOT** extend to `MENTAL_HEALTH` chronic records (grant-only) вҖ” a longitudinal psychiatric label is not operational information for a headmaster.
**C В· `working_impression` NOT `diagnosis` (R43):** the string `diagnos` appears in **no** column/enum/type/zod-key/label/route anything 0057 ships (grep-testable). Only structured clinical vocabulary in all of 4.4 is `chronic_condition_enum` (7 values, INCR-23). At 22 every clinical assertion is free text. No ICD/SNOMED/code-list/picker. `red_flags_screened` stays **free text** вҖ” structuring it into a checkable screen is an EMR feature. `escalation_triggers` is **inert**: stored, never evaluated.
**D В· vitals (R44/R45):** 5 measures + pain, fixed units (**no `unit` column** вҖ” a second fact that can disagree), all nullable with вүҘ1 required, plausibility bounds in zod as typo guards (temp 25вҖ“45, sys 50вҖ“260, dia 30вҖ“160, pulse 20вҖ“250, SpOвӮӮ 50вҖ“100, pain 0вҖ“10). **Append-only: no update, no delete, no void, no `updated_at`.** **ZERO derived alerting at 22** вҖ” cell colours/pills are presentation from a pure DB-free helper; trend deltas are arithmetic; anything that *acts* on a value is surveillance вҶ’ INCR-27.
**E В· рҹ”ҙ THE ATTENDANCE HOOK (22b) вҖ” writes into shipped Basic-tier code:** **R46** fires on **ADMIT and REFER, NEVER on DISCHARGE** вҖ” the 20-minute headache gets no `M` (every attendance claim on every surface attaches to an *admission*; a routine visit is not an attendance event, and it must not become a row every class teacher can read). **R47** ONE mark per student per day (R30 discharged вҖ” no per-period attendance), civil date Africa/Accra, **today only, never backdated**. **R48** multi-day needs **NO scheduler**: **PUSH** at disposition writes today (upgrading an already-taken `ABSENT`), **PULL** = the shared writer coerces on **INSERT only** when the student is under an open medical hold вҖ” so day 2/3/4 are marked the moment the teacher takes the register. One predicate `medicalHoldStudentIds()` = open admission covering the date **OR** open visit presented that date (which correctly handles the 07:30 clinic visit still open at the 08:00 register). INCR-25 extends the same function with the open-referral arm and no caller changes. **R49** the shared writer is `lib/attendance/mark.ts`, **`server-only` and emphatically NOT `"use server"`** (every export of a `"use server"` module is a remotely callable endpoint). (a) the downgrade guard is a **DB `setWhere`** on the existing `onConflictDoUpdate` вҖ” caller-agnostic by construction. (b) **рҹ”ҙ R49b LIVE DEFECT:** `saveAttendance` derives `absent` (вҶ’ parent SMS вҶ’ audit `after.absent`) from `d.entries`, the teacher's **input**. With the guard in place the row write is correctly blocked **and the mother still gets "Adwoa was marked absent" while Adwoa is on bed 3 in the school's own sickbay** вҖ” the exact harm this module exists to prevent, shipped by a guard that "worked". Fix: `.returning()` on each upsert; SMS + audit computed from **effective** statuses. (c) the **closed-term check MOVES INTO** the shared writer; the **edit-window lock STAYS** in `saveAttendance` (a teacher-register concept вҖ” a matron admitting at 14:00 into a 30-hour-old register must not be blocked), safe only because of R47. **R50** `reason_code='SICKBAY'` is **NOT teacher-pickable** (a teacher who could select it could forge a clinical assertion) вҖ” add `SICKBAY вҶ’ "In sickbay"` to the label map only. **Location, never condition** вҖ” a teacher who does not know stops chasing a child who cannot come. **R51** the `M` is **NEVER reverted** by the sickbay вҖ” not on discharge, not on error; correction is the existing co-signed `attendance_correction` flow only. Voiding cannot touch attendance **by construction** (void is legal only while `disposition IS NULL`, and only ADMIT/REFER write). вҡ пёҸ `decideCorrection` must **clear `reason_code`** when approving a change away from MEDICAL, else the row reads incoherently; and because coercion is INSERT-only, **the co-signed correction always wins**. **R52** closed term вҶ’ clinical write COMMITS, mark SKIPPED, reason `CLOSED_TERM`. **R53 рҹ”ҙ CLASSLESS:** skip the mark, **never block the visit** (a sick child is treated first), **never go silent** (honest line on the disposition card + `attendance_mark_skipped` audit row). `class_id` stays **NOT NULL** вҖ” relaxing a shipped Basic-tier constraint for a seed defect is backwards. **It IS a seed defect and it is fixed in 22b**: `db/seed/wassce.ts:223вҖ“237` creates 246 candidates with no class/house/residency (measured: non-WASSCE **28/28** classed, WASSCE **0/246**), so not one can receive an attendance row and Y. Aidoo cannot demo the headline integration; ~15 lines reusing the `wassce-mock.ts:133` class-upsert idiom, **scoped to the `SHS-2023-*` marker rows only**. **R54** the attendance write is **BEST-EFFORT and OUTSIDE the clinical transaction** вҖ” the visit is the medico-legal record and must survive an attendance subsystem having a bad day. The one place atomicity is deliberately rejected.
**F В· mode:** **R55** Mode C ADMIT refused at the **SERVER**, not hidden in the UI; bed board absent from the DOM. **R56** R6's deferred guard lands вҖ” reject вҶ’REFERRAL_ONLY while ANY admission is open, named error in the R11 grammar (open *visits* do not block; only beds-in-use do). **R57** `admission.is_isolation` **MUST equal** `bed.is_isolation` вҖ” isolation is a property of the CASE, so no judgment call and no overflow either way. **R58** three exclusivity invariants by **PARTIAL UNIQUE INDEX, not app check** (app checks lose the concurrent double-admit race): one open admission per bed В· per student В· one open visit per student. **R59** `occupiedBedIds` stops being `[]` вҶ’ the INCR-21 B5 reject path becomes reachable and gets a real **integration** test.
**G В· doctor consult (R60):** separate artefact; `clinician_name` **copied onto the row** (a locum/ER registrar is not the settings value, and the record must keep who actually said it); it is **hearsay with attribution** (render "recorded by {matron}"); **it cannot be a co-sign or a gate** вҖ” an unauthenticated external actor cannot be an authorisation subject (forward: INCR-24's `Doctor-ordered` MAR tag records **provenance, never permission**); append-only, corrected by a second row.
**H В· omit-not-fake (R61/R62/R63/R65):** OMITTED entirely вҖ” SCD protocol banner + `View care plan` В· `Sickle cell В· HbSS` chip В· **the queue's `No chronic flag` column (a false NEGATIVE вҖ” it asserts *safety* about a register the system cannot see; worse than a false zero)** В· the 4-row discharge checklist + `3 of 4 met` (per-condition templates вҶ’ 23) В· `NHIS В· active` В· `bed S-12-B` В· В§03 meds entirely В· В§05 entirely (notification log, HM card, follow-up, cross-links, immutable-close) В· today В§01 HM strip В· cluster-watch tile В· active-referrals tile В· **the triage `Routine` pill (R62 вҖ” a single-valued enum nobody sets is wrong the first time it matters; a hardcoded pill is an *unassessed clinical-urgency assertion*)** В· both print actions. **R63** discharge criteria = **free text** + `expected_discharge_at` + required `overnight_plan` (the "no silent overnight stays" rule preserved at 22; the parent half is 26). **R65** ONE honest attendance line in the В§04 disposition card, naming a **day** never periods, and it is where the R52/R53 skip warning lives.
**I В· R64 four more BUILD_STACK amendments** (continuing INCR-21's six): (7) `vitals_json` вҶ’ `sickbay_vital_reading` rows (a JSON blob cannot carry per-reading `taken_by_user_id`, cannot be time-indexed, cannot be append-only). (8) **drop `sickbay_visits.discharged_at`** вҖ” superseded by `disposition_at` + the admission's `discharged_at`; two end-stamps for one fact can disagree. (9) `disposition_enum`вҶ’`sickbay_disposition`, new `sickbay_consult_mode` (module prefix, R1). (10) `parent_notified_at`/`tier_fired` are **NOT in 0057** вҖ” a `tier_fired` column with no chain to fire it is a stub (authored at 0060, built at 26). (11) **no generated `visit_ref`** вҖ” it encodes 3 facts already on the row in a format the surfaces contradict four ways; a pure formatter if a printed header needs it.
**вҡ–пёҸ Kofi вҹӮ Lucy divergences вҖ” KOFI RULES (spec authority), reasons recorded:** (1) **trigger** вҖ” Lucy read "admission only" off the surfaces; **R46 adds REFER** (a student at Asankrangwa Govt. Hospital is definitively not in class and definitively not unauthorised-absent вҖ” precisely what the 5th status exists for). The surface simply never draws a referral. (2) **multi-day** вҖ” Lucy proposed *backfill-on-discharge*; **R48's push+pull wins** because backfill leaves the register showing wrong data *during* the admission and only corrects it at the end. (3) **0057 size** вҖ” Lucy mapped 6 tables + 3 enums (separate assessment + criterion tables); **Kofi's 4 tables + 2 enums wins** (assessment folds into the visit row as columns; the structured criterion instance needs per-condition templates вҶ’ INCR-23, R63).
**рҹ”’ Lucy's 11 ADJACENCY leaks (A1вҖ“A11) вҖ” rendering decisions no column list catches; all binding:** **A1** the bed tile printing `SCD` beside a name вҶ’ **condition removed, duration only** (the map's central ruling). **A2** the live tile `A. Mensa В· bed 3 В· SCD crisis` вҶ’ name+bed for ONE patient, **no names at all above one**. **A4** the SCD banner leaks **twice вҖ” by name AND by drug** (`hydroxyurea` вҮ’ sickle cell). **A6** the queue printing the complaint (`Menstrual cramps`) beside a name **on a bench-side screen** (independent reason the `Print day sheet` action is omitted). **A7 рҹ”ҙ `attendance_record.note` is the module's ONLY outbound leak path into the Basic tier** вҶ’ write `null` or a fixed non-clinical string, **never** the complaint or impression. **A11** physical shoulder-surfing is the whole justification вҖ” recorded so a future implementer does not "restore" the condition line as a helpful touch.
**AC (Quinn):** **H1вҖ“H18** (the attendance hook вҖ” the highest-value tests in the module; H6 is the R49b SMS regression, H8 the no-scheduler multi-day proof, H11 classless-must-not-throw, H14 the co-signed correction winning, H17 the full shipped attendance suite passing untouched, H18 zero active students classless after seed) В· **V1вҖ“V12** lifecycle В· **Z1вҖ“Z5** authz (Z2: ADMIN's **flight payload** carries no clinical field) В· **W1вҖ“W4** working-impression ceiling В· **T1вҖ“T5** vitals В· **M1вҖ“M8** mode В· **D1вҖ“D5** consult В· **O1вҖ“O4** omit-not-fake (O4: `===` character-exact copy comparison, the INCR-21 method) В· **S1вҖ“S4** structural (**S2: the from-empty replay must confirm `sickbay_visit_tenant_uk` is emitted BEFORE the three composite FKs targeting it вҖ” the 0033 hazard INSIDE a single migration**).
**рҹ”¶ OWNER-ESCALATE (all defaulted, none blocking):** **E4** triage vocabulary вҶ’ omit at 22. **E5 рҹ”” a communication REGRESSION the owner should see coming:** today a student in a sickbay bed is marked ABSENT and her mother gets *"Adwoa was marked absent"*; after 22b she is marked Medical and her mother gets **nothing**, because D8 keeps parents out of sickbay until the Tier-2 chain at **INCR-26**. Default **accept** (silence beats a false accusation) вҖ” flagged so it is a decision, not a surprise. **E6** ADMIN cannot read a visit record until INCR-23; for a single-admin school the account that pays for the system cannot open sickbay clinical records for one increment. Default accept вҖ” the honest escape is that the *role* carries clinical read, so an admin who really runs the sickbay assigns themselves MATRON. **E7** confirming R42 (mental-health grant-only at 23) since D2 was an owner decision.
**Also found:** shipped-copy defect `PROGRAMME_ABBR.GENERAL_SCIENCE = "GS"` contradicts all three surfaces (`SCI`) вҖ” one-line fix that also corrects the already-merged INCR-21 setup surface. `.cluster-note` is used but never defined in the visit-record file (take it from `schoolup-sickbay-setup.html:191`).

### INCR-22a+22b В· Build + gate outcomes (PR #174 вҖ” awaiting owner merge) вҖ” вҡ пёҸ prod deploy: paste `0056` **then** `0057`
- **Commits:** Wells 0057 `0e0d1ad` В· 22a visit path `03e0cf1` В· 22b attendance hook `95ed619` В· gate rework `968d937` В· tx un-nesting `e08c042`. **22a+22b merge TOGETHER** (22a alone = an admission that doesn't excuse attendance). **22c still to come.**
- **Gates ALL GREEN:** Quinn **GREEN** (H1вҖ“H18 + V/Z/W/T/M/D/O/S; **H5/H6/H8/H14 mutation-proven** вҖ” reverting the R49b fix turns 4 checks red *and emits a real SMS*; Z2 proven from **served HTML with a MATRON positive control**, 9/9 tokens vs ADMIN 0/9, so the negative isn't vacuous; closed 2 gaps the shipped harness left вҖ” H8's discharge-closes-the-hold and M5's live Mode-C ADMIT refusal; 617 tests). Dex **APPROVE** (dependency direction **correct and confined**; client/server seam **structural**; portability clean; mutation-killed 3 guards itself). Sarah **CLEAR-TO-MERGE** (**12-vector attacker probe as the non-superuser `omnischools_app`** with a positive control: unset GUC В· forged school id В· claimed-parent session В· cross-tenant INSERT Г—4 В· **row relocation in BOTH directions** В· cross-tenant DELETE В· foreign-parent composite FK вҖ” all refused; `tenant_isolation` carries `WITH CHECK` as well as `USING`, so a school cannot *export* a row either).
- **рҹ”ҙ The R49b live defect вҖ” found by Kofi, fixed and mutation-proven:** `saveAttendance` derived the absent list (вҶ’ **parent SMS** вҶ’ audit) from `d.entries`, the teacher's **input**. With the D4 guard in place the row write is correctly blocked **and the mother of an admitted student still gets "Adwoa was marked absent" while Adwoa is on bed 3 in the school's own sickbay** вҖ” the exact harm the module exists to prevent, shipped by a guard that "worked". Now derived from `.returning()` (effective statuses).
- **рҹ”ҙ Gate BLOCKERS found + closed (`968d937`):** **R1** a *"Referral note (optional)"* textarea was collected вҶ’ parsed вҶ’ written into the audit `after`, but **no column stored it** вҖ” a matron's referral reasoning invisible forever, on the increment whose premise is "the visit IS the medico-legal record". Closed by **deletion** (Refer is now one-click; the zod key removed so a crafted POST can't smuggle it into `audit_log` either; no column вҮ’ no second prod paste; the surface never drew it вҖ” 22a invented it). **R2** the H6 block went red **1-in-14** on an unchanged tree. Root-caused a **real UTC-midnight rollover** in the verifier (`civilDate()` is UTC, host is BST вҶ’ the civil day turns at 01:00 local; the script pinned `today` at module load while the actions compute at call time), **reproduced deterministically** with a new fake-clock harness (red at 2500/2700/2800/3200 ms leads, green at 2600/4000) and fixed (pin once at `main()`, wait out a rollover under 60s, assert the day didn't turn). Shipped as `pnpm db:verify-sickbay-attendance-rollover`.
- **рҹҹ  STANDING WATCH ITEM вҖ” the 1-in-14 observation is NOT fully explained.** Dex disproved the rollover as *its* cause: the failing run's H5 stamp was `2026-07-21T23:32:23Z` вҖ” **28 minutes** before UTC midnight, not the ~3s window the mechanism needs вҖ” and under a rollover **H1 fails before H6 can** (H1/H4/H7 and both H5 checks were green in that log). The audit counters `{absent:1, marked:1, heldMedical:1}` were verbatim tool output yet are arithmetically unreachable for either save in that sequence. **Why it does not block:** the harm path no longer depends on any verifier вҖ” the downgrade guard is a **DB `setWhere`** (caller-agnostic by construction) and the writer set is pinned repo-wide by a mutation-killed test. **The discriminator:** if the H6 cluster reddens again **with `pinned == now`**, the rollover is exonerated and it becomes a genuine writer-side investigation. Do not close this without that evidence.
- **Structural guards added (all mutation-killed):** the set of files writing `attendanceRecords` is pinned to exactly `mark.ts` + `decideCorrection` (+ a raw-SQL-name check) В· `medical-hold.ts` is asserted to import **nothing** from `lib/attendance/` вҖ” the acyclicity is load-bearing because the reverse edge already exists (`visit-reads.ts` imports `civilDate`/`closedTermLabel`) and **INCR-25 is aimed at extending that exact function** В· the `diagnos` ceiling now sweeps the 22b files + `db/schema/sickbay.ts` + `0057_*.sql` + the prod paste, and `stripComments` handles trailing `//`/`--` (before this delta a `diagnosisCode: text(...) // вҖҰ` walked straight through вҖ” Dex verified) В· `KNOWN_APP_ROLES` validates `AUTH_DEV_ROLES` with a loud throw.
- **рҹҹў Post-gate fix (`e08c042`, Dex):** `auditSkip` opened its own `withSchool` **inside** the still-open one вҖ” holding a pool connection while acquiring another (postgres.js default max 10), the classic exhaustion-deadlock shape, and about to become the idiom for 23вҖ“28. The skip reason is now **returned out of the callback and audited after the tx resolves**: smaller diff, same guarantee (nothing is written in either skip branch, so there is no tx to preserve, and the audit stays outside so a failing insert can't downgrade a NAMED reason to `FAILED`).
- **рҹҹ  Sarah's advisories for INCR-23вҖ“28:** (1) **the clinical read gate lives at the CALL SITE, not in the read.** Correct today (one call site, gate above the fetch вҖ” so ADMIN's clinical query is never *issued*). At 23 the rule becomes **per-row** (`role вҲҲ READ || hasGrant(actor, student)`) which RLS cannot express, arriving exactly when her INCR-21 "every reader is privileged anyway" assumption dies. **Move the gate into the read function (or a `requireClinicalRead(schoolId, studentId)` seam) at 23, before there are three call sites** вҖ” the write path already models this with `authorizeClinicalWrite()`. (2) `attending_user_id`'s app-only tenancy guard (global `ref_user`, so the DB cannot check it вҖ” her INCR-21 advisory 2 landing exactly as predicted) **replicates** at 24's prescriber/standing-order pointers: extract one `assertSchoolClinician()` rather than copy-paste `holdsMatronRole`. (3) `referralOnlyGuard`/`planBedReconcile` surface bed numbers + occupancy to ADMIN/HEADMASTER config actions вҖ” occupancy only, unavoidable for the invariant; **at 23 the temptation to name the patient in that error must be refused**. (4) the writer-set pin is identifier-shaped вҖ” an aliased import evades it (the raw-SQL check still covers the back door).
- **рҹҹ  22c obligations:** **22c must NOT reuse `getVisitRecord`** вҖ” it returns complaints/impressions/vitals/consults, so per-row use on the board is simultaneously an NГ—9 round-trip **and** a Lucy-A6 adjacency leak (a complaint beside a name on a bench-side screen). 22c needs its own **field-limited reader** in the R41 signature shape. Also: 22c must absorb or re-point `/senior/sickbay/visits/new` (authored by 22a as the write path's only entry since the queue is 22c) so it does not survive as a second, unmapped route that bypasses the queue's guards.
- **рҹҹ  Still deferred to INCR-24** (all only bite once 0059's medication tables carry `(school_id, slot_id)`): `resetScheduleSlots` hard DELETE В· the `validateRoundOrdering` TOCTOU В· a slot-create action must refuse a second anchor В· `admitPatient` reads `getSickbayConfig` outside the tx (same TOCTOU shape) В· `medical-hold.ts`'s non-sargable `::date` casts + a missing `(school_id, student_id, admitted_at)` index (it runs on **every register save at every Senior school forever**).
- **рҹҺ« Out-of-scope defect spun off to its own ticket** (Quinn verified pre-existing by replaying at `f2a6439`, before any INCR-22 code): `pnpm db:verify-score-ledger` fails 3 assertions on already-merged Module 4.1 code вҖ” **a score batch containing an out-of-range cell commits its valid rows anyway** (a silent partial write on the ledger feeding WASSCE projections and report cards), and `setLedgerPath` accepts the unbuilt Path B. Same "standing red hides real regressions" pattern as the RLS-test drift fixed at INCR-21.
- **Honest omissions:** the queue's `No chronic flag` column (a false **NEGATIVE** вҖ” asserts a student is *safe* per a register that doesn't exist until 23) В· the SCD banner (leaks the condition **twice**, by name and by drug) В· chronic chips В· NHIS В· the triage `Routine` pill В· the discharge checklist В· `bed S-12-B` В· В§03 medications В· В§05 entirely. `attendance_record.note` is always `null` (A7 вҖ” the module's only outbound path into the Basic tier).

## INCR-22a+22b вң… MERGED (PR #174, `0e0d1ad`+`03e0cf1`+`95ed619`+`968d937`+`e08c042`) вҖ” sickbay visit + attendance-M hook В· migration 0057 В· вҡ пёҸ prod-paste `0056` then `0057` RUN by owner 2026-07-22

### INCR-22c В· Kofi rulings R68вҖ“R90 + AC (2026-07-22) В· Lucy map: `docs/senior/sickbay-today-surface-map.md` вҖ” the Today board В· **NO migration, NO prod-paste, NO split**
**Scope:** `today` В§01 (crumb/h1/lede В· live strip В· admitted block В· queue В· bed board) + **В§03 "Recent visits В· 24h"** вҖ” built as a SECTION of `/senior/sickbay/today`, not a second route (R75; `TODAY_PATH` is already every shipped 22a write's revalidation target вҖ” the route was pre-agreed in code). В§02 roundsвҶ’24, В§04 referralsвҶ’25, В§05 outbreakвҶ’27: **absent entirely**. Everything derives from 0056/0057; Q1 rides the `sickbay_visit_presented_idx (school_id, presented_at)` authored in 0057 with a comment anticipating exactly this read.
- **R68 the reader вҖ” `lib/sickbay/board-reads.ts`, `server-only`, ONE entry** `getSickbayBoard(schoolId, roles, now)`. **O(1) round trips is part of the contract** вҖ” ~4вҖ“6 selects, independent of row count; any per-row query fails the AC whatever it returns. **`now` is a PARAMETER, never `new Date()` inside the reader or a child component** вҖ” pinned once in `page.tsx` and threaded (grounded in the 22a R2 blocker: a clock read at module load vs call time went red 1-in-14 and cost a day; three components each calling `new Date()` can render a queue whose "oldest wait" predates its own oldest row).
- **R69/R87 the field ceiling вҖ” four DISJOINT row types, and the ceiling is now ONE sentence:** *the only clinical string anywhere in the board reader is `presenting_complaint`, on the queue projection only.* `SickbayQueueRow` {visitId, studentName, formLabel, houseName, studentCode, presentedAt, **complaint**} В· `SickbayWardPatient` {admissionId, visitId, bedNumber, isIsolation, studentName, formLabel, houseName, studentCode, admittedAt, admittedByName, expectedDischargeAt, latestVital{вҖҰ}, firstPainScore} В· `SickbayBedTile` {bedNumber, isIsolation, occupant: null | {studentName, formLabel, houseName, admittedAt}} В· `SickbayRecentVisitRow` {visitId, presentedAt, studentName, formLabel, houseName, disposition, dispositionAt}. Every type except the queue is **structurally incapable** of carrying a clinical assertion вҖ” A1 stops being a vigilance item.
- **R70 three guards, none of them a comment:** (1) **runtime key-set pin** вҖ” `Object.keys(row).sort()` equals a frozen list per type (TS interfaces erase at runtime; the returned object does not; mutation-killable). (2) **one SELECT per type** вҖ” no board type may be produced by mapping over another (`beds = ward.map(...)` is banned; that is how a clinical field arrives as a "harmless" spread). (3) **served-HTML token test with a POSITIVE control** (Quinn's Z2 method).
- **рҹ”ҙ R87 (SUPERSEDES the narrative clause of R69/R85) вҖ” `.ab-line`'s clinical prose comes OFF the board.** `SickbayWardPatient` loses `workingImpression`/`hydrationStatus`/`plan`: not selected, not returned, not rendered. **Lucy's A13 wins.** Kofi's own words: *"I deleted three characters (`SCD`) from the bed tile and kept `Mild vaso-occlusive pain crisis В· вҖҰ Hydroxyurea continued` eight lines above it, on the same screen, for the same readers. **A rule that survives only where the string is short is not a rule.**"* Three grounds: (a) his **own R76 test applied consistently** вҖ” the A6 exception is bought by *operational necessity*, and narrative prose supports no decision the record one click away doesn't; (b) it is an **A4 leak by construction** вҖ” free-text `plan`/`hydrationStatus` are exactly where a matron types drug names, and `hydroxyurea` вҮ’ sickle cell, so `.ab-line` is the omitted SCD banner restored in user-typed form on the landing page; (c) **A8 justified it on the role gate, and the role gate is not the threat** вҖ” it decides who logs in, not who is standing behind the matron at a bench-side screen (A11). *"A8 answered the wrong question and I ratified it."* **Replacement (slot + dashed border kept):** `Expected discharge **{t}**` В· `В· **reassessment overdue**` (gold, when passed and `discharged_at` null) В· trailing `Open record вҶ’`. The line **always renders** (supersedes R85's "no assessment вҮ’ no line"). **`.ab-vitals` SURVIVES** вҖ” Lucy's A14: the glance-check on a patient ten metres away is a genuine patient-safety instrument, and removing it would push the matron to open full records *more* often, which is worse for exposure overall. The pain trend survives in the Pain tile's own sub-line, where the surface put it.
- **R88 the gate STANDS unamended.** Still `SICKBAY_CLINICAL_READ_ROLES = [HEADMASTER, MATRON]`; ADMIN gets `ClinicalRestricted` and the board is **never fetched**. The page still carries the queue `complaint` (Class 1, Class 4 when reproductive вҖ” `Menstrual cramps`) and the Class-3 vitals grid. **Pre-emptively refused:** "the narrative is gone, so give ADMIN a counts-only board" вҖ” that is the third read tier R80 rejected; R41 reserves the field-limited tier for INCR-28. вҡ пёҸ **`SickbayBedTile` is now very close to what 28's housemaster reader needs вҖ” that is a TRAP, not a convenience.** 28 authors its own narrower reader and must not import from `board-reads.ts`.
- **R81 Sarah's advisory TAKEN for the board** вҖ” the gate moves INTO the read: `getSickbayBoard` returns `null` for a non-clinical reader, role check as the **first statement before any query is issued** (preserving the property that makes Z2 strong). At 23 the per-row rule (`role вҲҲ READ || hasGrant`) is added *inside*, where roles are already in scope. **`getVisitRecord` keeps its call-site gate at 22c** вҖ” its `null` already means *not of this school* вҶ’ `notFound()`; overloading it with *forbidden* turns ADMIN's honest panel into a 404 and deletes the E6 escape. Converting it needs a discriminated result and 23 has the second input (grants) to justify the shape. Quinn pins it meanwhile: **every file importing a clinical reader must also reference `SICKBAY_CLINICAL_READ_ROLES`** (the mutation-killed writer-set-pin idiom).
- **рҹ”ҙ R76 В§03's complaint column comes OFF вҖ” corroborated INDEPENDENTLY by Lucy (A12).** A6 buys the complaint on the *queue* with a triage necessity a **closed** visit does not have; nothing on a retrospective log is being decided, and the matron needs to *find* a row, which time+name+form+House+pill does. Lucy's added evidence: three of the surface's six strings in that cell aren't complaints but impressions/readings/condition names (`malaria RDT negative`, `sickle cell pain crisis`, `asthma chronic`, `pain 7/10`) вҖ” **six legible at once vs the queue's three**. `.v-action` also dropped (A12b вҖ” per-row drug re-identification, and half-unbacked anyway). вҡ пёҸ **Kofi flags this as the ruling most likely to be "helpfully" reverted by a future implementer who sees an empty-looking log вҖ” say A11 in the PR.**
- **R75 В§03 window = ROLLING 24h from `now` on `presented_at`, NOT the civil date.** The log's job is shift handover, and a civil-date window is **empty at 06:00** вҖ” exactly when the incoming matron needs last night's 19:40 referral. One timestamp, one predicate, sargable. **R75b:** the window is NOT widened to catch stale open visits; instead 22c enriches the shipped open-visit collision error (`"This student already has an open sickbay visit."`) to the R11 grammar вҖ” name the day, link the record вҖ” because now that a board exists there is nowhere to go looking. **R77** disposition pills `Discharged {HH:MM}` / `Admitted` / `Referred` + AUTHORED neutral **`Open`**; `ON_WARD_DISCHARGED` still reads `Admitted` (R36 makes the disposition immutable; the bed board 200px above answers "still on a bed" authoritatively). Open visits ARE included (an IN_PROGRESS visit appears nowhere else on the board). Order `presented_at` desc. **R78** voided visits excluded from В§03 and from every counter вҖ” a log row naming a student who was never seen is a false clinical adjacency, and a counter including it over-reports care delivered.
- **R71/R72/R73/R74 В§01:** bed tile = `Bed 03` В· `A. Mensa` В· `F1 В· Slessor` В· `05h 31m`, condition slot **kept but re-toned** `text-terra`вҶ’`text-navy-3` (a duration is not an alarm) В· queue = 4 columns, complaint is the single named exception, `Begin visit` writes `started_at` **then** navigates (a nav-only button would leave R33's wait clock running on a student being treated) and renders only for writers while the row still renders for a HEADMASTER (affordance filter, never a data filter) В· **A2 one-name rule:** 1 admission вҶ’ `**{I}. {Surname}** В· bed {n}`; **>1 вҶ’ `{n} on the ward`, NO names at all**; 0 вҶ’ no meta В· **counter honesty:** `0 / 8 beds` is a **known** zero and renders (R27's false zero was `0/8` when no admission table existed), but with zero active beds render `0` with **no `/ M` denominator** (a capacity the school never configured is the false-zero shape again) В· empty queue renders `0` with **no meta at all** (`avg wait 0 min` asserts a measured wait for a patient who doesn't exist) В· **partition invariant: the breakdown terms SUM to the total.**
- **R89 (AMENDS R71) вҖ” NO Mode-C panel on the board.** Kofi: *"I reached rung 2 of the ladder (reuse the shipped `MODE_C_CAPACITY_PANEL`) without asking rung 1."* **Setup is a decision surface** вҖ” the panel is new information when an admin is choosing a mode. **The board is a daily operational surface** вҖ” a permanent panel explaining the school has no beds is noise by week two, and an explanatory panel where a card was is a soft placeholder. Mode C is not bare (2-tile strip + queue promoted to full width + the 24h log). **Empty by design means empty.** What replaces the bed card: **nothing.** вң… **ADOPTED вҖ” the `configured === false` notice** (one dashed panel above the strip, every reader): `Sickbay not set up yet вҖ” declare your school's mode in **Sickbay setup**.` This is R25 landing correctly вҖ” a coalesced `REFERRAL_ONLY` is NOT a declared Mode C, and without it a FULL-mode school that never ran setup sees no bed board and concludes the product doesn't do beds. **Orthogonal to mode**, renders whatever the coalesced mode says, disappears when setup is saved.
- **R90 the surface's own numbers and weekday are WRONG вҖ” derive both.** Tile 3's `5 В· 3 discharged В· 1 admitted В· 1 awaiting` **contradicts В§03's own table** (4 discharges) and excludes the three students standing in its own queue; the correct demo value is **8 = 4 discharged В· 1 admitted В· 3 awaiting**. First live proof that a *drawn* number loses to a *derived* one (spec wins on logic, HTML wins on presentation) вҖ” and exactly what R74's partition invariant exists to catch. **`Wed 14 May 2026` is a THURSDAY (Lucy F7)** вҖ” the h1 date derives `EEE d MMM yyyy` from the pinned `now`, and **the string must not appear in any expected-copy fixture** or O4's character-exact method would enshrine the error.
- **R82/R83/R84 routes & nav:** `/senior/sickbay/visits/new` is **KEPT and re-pointed** (it bypasses nothing вҖ” the queue doesn't create visits and every guard lives in `createVisit`); the board head's `New visit` links to it, its crumb becomes `Sickbay В· Today В· New visit`, and `safeRevalidate(TODAY_PATH)` is **already shipped** вҖ” verify, don't re-author. **`Admit patient` is OMITTED from the board head** вҖ” an admission is a *disposition* of an in-progress visit (R35) requiring `started_at` + complaint + impression (R34), so a top-level button is either a second write path skipping the preconditions or `New visit` with a misleading label: **omit-not-fake covers affordances, not just data.** Sidebar `Sickbay` re-points to `/senior/sickbay/today` (**row count unchanged**, no sub-nav); crumb convention `Sickbay`вҶ’setup (module root), `Today`вҶ’the board; `ClinicalRestricted` gains an optional `label` and keeps its setup link so a restricted ADMIN is never stranded.
- **R85 admitted block:** one per open admission ordered by `bedNumber`; class renamed `.adwoa-block`вҶ’`.admitted-block` (a CSS class named after a fabricated demo patient does not ship); `formLabel()` everywhere (the surface's `F1 General Arts` vs `F1 SCI` is drift); chronic tag absent; `.ab-vitals` Г—5 use the **visit record's** vocabulary (`Temp В· BP В· HR В· SpOвӮӮ В· Pain`) and the same `vitalSeverity()`; **a metric absent from the latest reading renders BLANK вҖ” never `вҖ”`, never `0`** (a dash in a vitals grid reads as "measured and normal" to a nurse).
- **AC:** **B1вҖ“B6** reader (B1 round-trips вүӨ6 and flat as the queue grows to 30 В· B3 frozen key-sets, mutation-killable В· **B4 is the headline: `ZZTOKENCOMP` exactly once, `ZZTOKENIMP` ZERO times anywhere including the flight payload, with the visit record as positive control вҖ” but see вҡ пёҸ below for WHICH check carries the payload half** В· B6 the SQL selects none of the five narrative columns) В· **Q1вҖ“Q7** queue В· **P1вҖ“P7** bed board (P3 Mode C: no bed markup **and no explanatory panel** В· P4 zero beds вҶ’ the setup link, `0 / 0` nowhere В· P6/P7 new) В· **N1вҖ“N7** counters (N5: tile 3 reads **8**, terms sum, the literal `5` is not an expected value anywhere) В· **L1вҖ“L9** В§03 (L4 the complaint token absent while name/form/House present В· L9 the enriched collision error) В· **G1вҖ“G5** gate (G1 ADMIN вҶ’ 200 + `ClinicalRestricted` + **zero** names/beds/complaints/impressions/counts, positive control В· G2 **no SQL issued** for ADMIN В· G5 repo-wide clinical-reader pin) В· **R1вҖ“R4** routes/nav В· **A-block** (overdue/expected/null-stamp branches; vitals grid always, clinical prose never) В· **O** omit register `===` character-exact, and **no fixture contains `Wed 14 May 2026`**.
- **вҡ пёҸ B4 CORRECTION (Quinn MINOR-1, post-gate) вҖ” "including the flight payload" is carried by B3 + B6, NOT by the served-HTML check.** Quinn proved it: add `workingImpression` to the ward projection **without rendering it** and **B3** (the runtime key-set pin) and **B6** (`JSON.stringify(board)` over the reader's own return) both go RED, while the served-HTML **B4 stays GREEN**. The reason is structural вҖ” this page's only client component is `<BeginVisitButton visitId={вҖҰ} />`, so the *only* prop that crosses the client boundary is a uuid; **server-component props never serialise into the flight payload at all**, so an unrendered leak is invisible to a check that greps the served document. The served check is still real (it catches a leak that *renders*) and it **becomes load-bearing the moment any clinical prop crosses a client boundary** вҖ” **INCR-23's per-row grants are the likely trigger**: the instant a row's clinical field is handed to a `"use client"` component, the flight payload starts carrying it and B4's served half is the only check that sees it. Until then, the payload guarantee is B3 + B6.
- **рҹ”¶ OWNER-ESCALATE (defaulted, none blocking):** **E8** the sidebar now lands ADMIN on `/today` where they see `ClinicalRestricted` вҖ” for a single-admin school that is the paying account opening Sickbay to a wall. Default accept (same escape as E6: clinical read travels with the MATRON role); the one-line variant is a role-conditional href sending ADMIN to setup. **E9** `Admit patient` gone from the board head (R83). **E10** authored copy for sign-off: `Open` В· `No visits in the last 24 hours.` В· `reassessment overdue` В· `{n} on the ward` В· `Sickbay not set up yet вҖ” declare your school's mode in Sickbay setup.` В· `Expected discharge {t}` В· `Open record вҶ’` В· the enriched collision error.

### INCR-22c В· Build + gate outcomes (вң… **MERGED**, PR #175) вҖ” рҹҸҒ **CLOSES MODULE 4.4's TRUNK** В· NO migration, NO prod-paste
- **Commits:** impl `92d0aec` В· gate rework `a58002e` В· Sarah ADV-2/ADV-3 `610bb8e`. Files: `lib/sickbay/{board-reads,board-copy,board-copy.test}.ts`, `app/(app)/senior/sickbay/today/page.tsx`, `components/sickbay/begin-visit-button.tsx`, `scripts/verify-sickbay-board.ts`, + touched `sidebar.tsx`, `clinical-restricted.tsx`, `sickbay-visit.ts`, `visits.ts`, `visit-copy.test.ts`. **658 tests**, `/senior/sickbay/today` = 906 B of client JS.
- **Gates ALL GREEN:** Quinn **GREEN** (**10 mutations across 7 runs, all killed**; no vacuous tests вҖ” every negative paired with a positive control in the same run; independently reconstructed the RSC flight stream by joining every `self.__next_f.push` chunk so a token split across a chunk boundary cannot produce a false pass). Dex **APPROVE** (gate structurally first; `board-reads.ts` has exactly ONE runtime export so there is no second door; O(1) flat; seam structural; portability clean). Sarah **CLEAR-TO-MERGE** (full attacker-path enumeration; **bed *ids* are unreachable in EVERY mode** вҖ” the reader selects `bedNumber`, never `id`, so no bed UUID can be serialised anywhere).
- **рҹ”ҙ Dex R1 вҖ” a guard that suppressed its own backstop вҶ’ FIXED (`a58002e`):** `isQueued({ ...v, voidedAt: null }, now)` hardcoded the flag to satisfy a type, so R78 ("a voided visit appears on no surface, in no counter") rested **entirely** on one SQL `isNull()` вҖ” and the literal silenced the one downstream check that would catch its removal. В§03 and the counters carried no void check at all. Now selects `voidedAt` and calls `isQueued(v, now)`. **Mutation-proven with an elegant signature:** delete the SQL predicate and the queue arm stays GREEN while the В§03/counter arm goes RED вҖ” that asymmetry *is* the proof the in-memory backstop is live, where the old form would have killed both arms together and told you nothing.
- **рҹ”ҙ Quinn MINOR-1 вҖ” our own AC text over-claimed:** adding `workingImpression` to the ward projection **without rendering it** turns B3 and B6 red but leaves **B4 green**, because the page's only client prop is `{visitId}` and server-component props never serialise вҖ” a field reaching the reader but never the JSX never enters the document. The mutant still dies, so B4-as-a-composite is not theatre, but **the payload guarantee is carried by B3 (runtime key-set pin) + B6 (SQL column check), not by the served check**. Sarah's framing of why the composite holds: **B6 is a DENYLIST, B3 is an ALLOWLIST** вҖ” B3 generalises to columns B6's name list has never heard of. вҡ пёҸ The served check **becomes** load-bearing the moment a clinical prop crosses a client boundary вҖ” INCR-23's per-row grants are the likely trigger.
- **рҹ”ҙ Sarah ADV-2 вҖ” the abbreviation tier had NO runtime pin вҶ’ FIXED (`610bb8e`):** the abbreviation IS a disclosure tier (A2/R73), but `BOARD_ROW_KEYS` could not distinguish an abbreviated `studentName` from a full one вҖ” the field name was identical across all four types. **Deleting `initials(` from the queue or В§03 projection would have shipped full student names to a bench-side screen with every gate still green** (B3 same key set, B6 not a narrative column, B4 wrong tokens). Renamed `SickbayWardPatient.studentName` вҶ’ **`studentFullName`**, making the tier compile-checked; it immediately surfaced **two call sites a grep had missed**.
- **рҹ”ҙ Sarah ADV-3 вҖ” the always-run gate evidence was satisfied by an IMPORT вҶ’ FIXED (`610bb8e`):** the assertion compared `indexOf("SICKBAY_CLINICAL_READ_ROLES")` (first occurrence = the import, ~L47) against the first `withSchool(` (~L204), so it passed on import ordering and **would still pass with the gate deleted outright**. Now matches the gate EXPRESSION; mutation-proven red. вҡ пёҸ Sarah's structural note: the behavioural half (G2) lives in a DB-backed script and **this repo has NO CI** (`.github/workflows` does not exist), so it runs only when someone runs it.
- **рҹҹў Dex A3 вҶ’ closed better than asked:** the O(1) guard counted `db.transaction` calls, i.e. **transactions, not statements** вҖ” blind to a per-row `tx.select` added *inside* an existing `withSchool` callback, which is exactly INCR-23's per-student chronic-lookup shape ("just add it to the ward query's callback"). Counting at the driver turned out cheap, so it now asserts **statement** count is flat (5 вҶ’ 5 for 31 rows).
- **Also fixed:** four divergent `A. Mensa` implementations collapsed to one exported `initials()` applied in the **reader** (so the type carries the tier), with the ward's full name the one documented exception В· `disposeVisit`/`addVitals` gained `safeRevalidate(TODAY_PATH)` so "the board revalidates" is a checkable rule (`assessVisit`'s omission is now a *named* exception grounded in R87) В· the queue action cell regained the surface's `text-align:right`.
- **рҹҹ  Sarah ADV-1 (design, back to Lucy/Kofi вҖ” NOT code):** A2 suppresses names above one admitted patient on tile 1, but one `AdmittedBlock` per admission renders ~100px below with the **full** name and vitals each. With four admitted, tile 1 says `4 on the ward` while four names and four temperatures stack underneath. Every block is individually ratified (A13 stripped the prose, A14 kept the grid, the surface prints `.ab-name` in full) вҖ” but the harm A2 exists to prevent is rendered anyway. Cheapest mitigation if wanted: collapse to a summary above 2 admitted, full blocks behind a click. No new reader, no new type.
- **рҹҹ  Carried to INCR-23 (Sarah's list вҖ” this is where her INCR-21 "every reader is privileged anyway" assumption DIES):** (1) **a grant cannot help someone the route rejects** вҖ” `requireSchoolRole(SICKBAY_ROLES)` refuses HOUSEMASTER before the reader is called, so 23 must either widen the module gate (making the reader's gate the only boundary) or author its own route. **Decide deliberately; do not discover it.** (2) **push the grant into SQL as an `EXISTS` in the WHERE**, inside the same `withSchool` tx вҖ” never over-fetch-then-filter-in-TS (the row is materialised before it is authorised) and never a per-row `hasGrant` (the N+1 R68 forbids); keep the coarse role check as the literal first statement so the ADMIN-zero-SQL property survives. (3) **the client boundary takes scalars or a separately-pinned view type вҖ” NEVER a reader row** (`<X row={row} />` ships every field into the flight payload regardless of what the JSX renders). (4) **`getSickbayBoard`'s signature breaks at 23** вҖ” `roles: readonly string[]` cannot express `hasGrant(actor, student)`; take it to `{id, roles}` or derive internally. (5) **read-side audit becomes mandatory**, deduped per (actor Г— student Г— day), grant expiry evaluated server-side per request and never cached in a session claim. (6) **R88's "don't import `SickbayBedTile`" warning names INCR-28 but NOT 23 вҖ” and 23 is the nearer risk.** 23 needs its own adjacency pass from Lucy; the board's rulings must not be re-litigated from it.
- **рҹҹ  Housekeeping (non-blocking):** a 5th/6th `shortName` still live in 22a/22b code (`visit-reads.ts:62`, `config.ts:268`) вҖ” the import direction is wrong-way, so move `initials()` to `defaults.ts` when 23 touches those files В· **the board harness creates its fixtures BEFORE the fetch it depends on, so any failure strands them** and poisons the next run (this cost real time during the gate; it also needs a running dev server, and `SERVED_ROLE=ADMIN` needs a server started with `AUTH_DEV_ROLES=ADMIN`) В· orphaned `audit_log` rows accumulate because both harnesses purge only the entity ids they name В· the repo is **not** Prettier-clean (193 files under `lib/**`) and nothing enforces it вҖ” one `pnpm format` commit + `format:check` in CI, or delete the script.
- **вҡ пёҸ PROD DEPLOY: NONE for 22c.** But Sarah's closing note: since this closes the trunk, **confirm `prod-paste-0056-sickbay-spine.sql` and `prod-paste-0057-sickbay-visit.sql` were actually run** вҖ” if either was missed, the whole sickbay trunk (visits, vitals, admissions, consults) leaks across schools, **and 22c is the surface that would put it on a screen.**
