## INCR-23 В· Chronic register вҖ” the third RLS boundary

### Interposed: PR #176 security hotfix (вң… MERGED, off `main`, folded into `senior-feat`)
A live PII leak found while mapping this increment, unrelated to sickbay but directly upstream of it. `requireSchool()` authenticated and resolved a school but did **no role check**, and 62 of the 82 `app/(app)` pages are gated by nothing else; accepting a PARENT invite creates a real `role_assignment`, so a claimed parent could read any student's blood group, allergies, conditions, medications and emergency contact вҖ” and `updateStudent` would have let them **overwrite** it. `requireSchool` is now staff-only by default with one greppable opt-in (`allowNonStaff`, used solely by the INCR-19b parent statement PDF). **Why it matters here:** the 19a parent boundary did not catch it because staff pages read under `withSchool`, leaving `app.current_parent_user` unset so `parent_deny`'s permit-by-default clause (`pu IS NULL OR вҖҰ`) let the row through. **That is exactly the polarity hazard R112 inverts** вҖ” and it is now a demonstrated one, not a theoretical one.
- Also shipped: a **guard-ordering invariant** (`lib/auth/app-shell-guard.test.ts`) вҖ” every `page.tsx` under `app/(app)` and `route.ts` under `app/api` that opens a tenant transaction must await a `require*` guard first; machine-to-machine exemptions are an explicit list and must each prove a fail-closed secret check before reading. Gate lesson recorded for every future guard test: **assert the CONSEQUENCE, not only the CONDITION** (Quinn kept the pinned `if`, deleted its `redirect`, and all 668 tests stayed green while the leak reopened) and **read comment-stripped source** (Dex found a guard name matching inside prose вҖ” a false PASS, the dangerous direction).
- рҹҹ  **Open, and it collides with this increment's premise:** every staff role currently reads *and edits* `student_health_record` (blood group, allergies, conditions, medications) with **no read audit**. INCR-23 cannot honestly call the chronic register "admin-private" while that page shows overlapping fields to any teacher. Ticketed, not fixed here. Also open: `isFinanceOnly(["BURSAR","PARENT"])` is `false`, so a bursar who accepts a parent invite escapes finance confinement.

### Owner decisions вҖ” ANSWERED (these close E15вҖ“E19 and the D-series; build to them)
- **D1 clinical narrative вҶ’ STORE IT.** Owner consciously accepts special-category health data under Ghana's DPA 2012.
- **D2 clinical read вҶ’ MATRON + HEADMASTER default; ADMIN grant-only.** (Unchanged; R116 carves `MENTAL_HEALTH` out of the Headmaster's half.)
- **D3 NHIS вҶ’ IN**, shape unsettled вҶ’ **INCR-25**. Confirms R127's omission at 23 (storing it now pre-commits the wrong shape; the card in the referral log is the *mother's*).
- **D4 attendance-M вҶ’ a teacher save cannot downgrade a sickbay-written `MEDICAL`;** correction only via co-signed `attendance_correction`. (Shipped in 22b as a DB-level `setWhere` guard.)
- **D5.1 retention вҶ’ 7 years post-exit, configurable per school in settings; STORE THE SETTING, BUILD NO PURGE AT 23, SOFTEN THE UI CLAIM.** This is Kofi's E15 recommended default with one addition: the setting is real and school-configurable now, the machinery is not. **Applies to all three objects** вҖ” `sickbay_chronic_read` rows, chronic entries after exit, and рҹ”ҙ `audit_log` rows carrying care-plan before/after snapshots (R103 makes the audit log a clinical record store; the owner had never been asked about that table). The save-bar copy keeps its append-only half **verbatim** and drops the 7-year assertion until a purge job exists вҖ” asserting a retention policy the repo cannot perform is omit-not-fake in reverse.
- **D5.2 controlled-substance register вҶ’ IN SCOPE, brief.** INCR-24 (dispensing/administration), not 23 вҖ” 23 stores a prescription *schedule*, never an administration.
- **D5.3 N&MC witness вҶ’ MANDATORY FOR CONTROLLED SUBSTANCES ONLY**, with a documented single-signature override. The witness must be **a real user in this school**, never free text. INCR-24.
- **E18 / R116 вҶ’ CONFIRMED grant-only, invisible by default.** The Headmaster sees 5 of 6 with **no signal a sixth exists**. Baked into `chronic_entry_ids` and the prod paste, so it had to be ruled before 23a вҖ” it now is.
- **E16 вҶ’ adopt the recommendation** (default access = MATRON + HEADMASTER; copy corrected from four roles to two; School Nurse folds into `MATRON`; Deputy Head (Welfare) reachable by grant). **E17 вҶ’ omit all three bulk exports**, rule them as a named later slice; `Print dorm copy` still ships at 23b. **E19 вҶ’ refuse the `Senior prefect` grant row.** **E20** authored copy accepted.

### Kofi rulings R91вҖ“R127 (2026-07-22) В· Lucy map: `docs/senior/sickbay-chronic-register-surface-map.md`
**Split: 23a / 23b, ONE migration (0058), ONE prod paste, one milestone branch.** The seam is *the day a non-clinical reader can see health data*. **23a** = 0058 + the `staff_grant_scope` boundary + `withStaffScope` + the verifier + В§01/В§02/В§03 + entry/med writes + the read-audit write + the debts to 22 + the `resetScheduleSlots` reconcile fix. **23b** = В§04 grants + `grantAccess`/`revokeAccess` + the widened route + the scoped projections + `Print dorm copy`. Unlike 22a/22b, **23a alone is a safe, honest, shippable state** вҖ” it is exactly D2's default with no grant issuable. 23b branches independently off the milestone head, **never stacked** (orphan-PR rule).

**A В· the register's model** вҖ” **R91** `sickbay_chronic_entry`, one row per (student Г— condition), NOT columns on `student_health_record` (whose `student_id` is globally `.unique()`, so SCD **and** asthma is inexpressible); the shipped table stays the 1:1 bio baseline, not migrated, not dual-written. **R92** module-wide `sickbay_` prefix. **R93** 0058 = 2 enums + 4 tables, nothing else. **R94** `chronic_condition` = BUILD_STACK L346 verbatim (7 values); the no-EMR ceiling is *enforced by* `OTHER` + free-text detail, never a migration; R43's `diagnos` sweep extends to every 23 file. вҡ пёҸ named ceiling: `MENTAL_HEALTH` is a **security discriminator** (R116), so the carve-out is only as good as the matron's classification вҖ” the entry form must state the consequence at the point of choice. **R95** status is THREE values (`STABLE|MONITOR|ACTIVE_CRISIS`); **`REFERRAL_MANAGED` is NOT a status** вҖ” as an enum value it forces a referral-managed student *in crisis* to choose, and crisis wins, silently erasing "we do not treat this on-site" at the one moment it matters. Consequence (the R90 shape again): the drawn counts are wrong; derived they are `All 6 В· crisis 1 В· monitor 2 В· stable 3`, with `Referral-managed` a **second-axis overlay pill, not a partition term**. **R96** `on_site_treatable` + `referral_managed` are independent NOT NULL booleans; `MENTAL_HEALTH вҮ’ (false,true)` is a **DB CHECK** (product policy, not per-school judgement; J3 forbids *cross-table* triggers, not a single-row CHECK). **R97** NO protocol-step table вҖ” `emergency_protocol` is ONE text column in the matron's own words; the terracotta frame is kept, the five numbered cards become her paragraphs; **do not write a prose parser to reconstruct the numbering.**
- **рҹ”ҙ R98 В· THE HEADLINE вҖ” the dorm-side card is a SEPARATELY AUTHORED artefact, not a redaction of the care plan.** The surface proves it: protocol step 4 lists *priapism (boys)* and *OвӮӮ sat <95%*; the dorm card says *"severe pain В· fever В· breathlessness В· chest pain"*. Different strings for different readers, not one string truncated. So the entry carries **HM-tier columns** (`triggers`, `red_flags`, `first_action`) alongside the clinical tier. **Why it is load-bearing: it deletes the entire class of redaction bug.** There is nothing to redact, so a scope is a fixed pinnable key-set (R70's runtime key-set pin generalises straight on) rather than a substring judgement made at render time.
- **R99** `sickbay_chronic_med` = one row per (entry Г— drug Г— slot | PRN); `dose_label` is text; CHECK `is_prn XOR slot_id`; the grid is a **pivot** (presentation). Rejected: a `slot_doses jsonb` map (R64(7) вҖ” INCR-24's round query becomes a full scan) and a third `_dose` table. рҹ”ҙ `slot_id` FK is **RESTRICT, not SET NULL** вҖ” SET NULL silently orphans a dose from its round, i.e. a student quietly stops being dosed. **R100 рҹ”ҙ the `resetScheduleSlots` obligation MOVES FORWARD from 24 to 23a** вҖ” it is a hard DELETE that changes every slot id, so "Reset to defaults" would cascade against (or, under RESTRICT, hard-fail) every chronic dose in the school. The TOCTOU and slot-create anchor guard stay at 24. **R101** med-grid columns render from `getRoundSchedule()`; the surface's `13:00 Lunch` is demo drift and loses. **R102** `on_site_treatable = false вҮ’ zero med rows`, app-layer in the writer (J3). **R103** versioning is a **counter + the shipped audit log** вҖ” no version table, no superseded rows; `v4` is a number. вҡ пёҸ this makes `audit_log` a clinical record store (see D5.1). **R104** discharge criteria = one free-text column + a **prefill** into the shipped visit field; the structured checklist and `3 of 4 met` stay omitted (R63 closed with a smaller answer).

**B В· grants** вҖ” **R105** a grant is per **ENTRY**, not per student (a grant on "Adwoa's plan" silently widening to a future `MENTAL_HEALTH` entry is exactly what R116 exists to prevent). **R106** the grantee is a `ref_user`, NOT NULL; **a STUDENT or PARENT may never hold one** (the `Senior prefect` demo row is refused вҖ” R38 already ruled one student's identity as an *actor* inside another's clinical record); a non-user gets the **printed** dorm card, which is the doctrine already. Reuses shipped `isStaff()`. **R107** grants are explicit rows a matron created вҖ” **auto-EXPIRE yes, auto-GRANT no.** The note panel's *"grants auto-transfer to the new HM"* **loses**: six students' medical records landing on a man the day he changes job, with no matron decision and no audit event, is the boundary this increment exists to build. The *"auto-expired"* half **wins**, made real by one nullable `house_id`: live iff `houses.hm_user_id = grantee AND student.house_id = grant.house_id`. One column, no new mechanism. **R108** scope enum is THREE values (`FULL_PLAN|PARTIAL|DIRECTIVE`); the surface's nine labels are not nine scopes (`Removed` is `revoked_at IS NOT NULL`; six others return the same projection and differ only in the matron's words). `REFERRAL_ONLY` вҶ’ **`DIRECTIVE`** (collides with `sickbay_mode_enum.REFERRAL_ONLY` *and* `referral_managed`) вҖ” BUILD_STACK amendment #11. **рҹ”ҙ R109** `DIRECTIVE` reads exactly ONE field and it lives **on the grant row** (`directive_note`, CHECK-enforced): the grantee sees student name + that sentence and **nothing from the entry at all** вҖ” not the condition, not the pill, not the colour. The narrowest tier is therefore *structurally incapable* of leaking. Three matron-authored strings live on a grant (`scope_label`, `reason`, `directive_note`) вҖ” do not collapse them. **R110** append-only: revoke never deletes; a scope change is revoke + re-grant, never an UPDATE. **R111** grant/revoke is **MATRON-only** вҖ” not HEADMASTER, not ADMIN (R39's split repeats: the Head reads but never authors).

**C В· the third boundary (the novel work)** вҖ” **рҹ”ҙ R112 DB-enforced, RESTRICTIVE, on `app.current_staff_user`, and DENY-BY-DEFAULT вҖ” the one clause that does NOT mirror 19a.** One `SECURITY DEFINER STABLE` function `chronic_entry_ids(school, su)` in `policies.sql` (never the migration) unioning (a) default clinical readers (`MATRON` вҶ’ all; `HEADMASTER` вҶ’ all except `MENTAL_HEALTH`) and (b) every entry with a live grant to `su`. Four `AS RESTRICTIVE FOR ALL TO public` policies named `staff_grant_scope`. **Polarity:** `USING (bypass OR (su IS NOT NULL AND <rule>))` versus the parent family's permit-by-default `pu IS NULL OR <rule>` вҖ” safe there because those tables' default audience *is* all staff; **the chronic tables have no default audience.** Once the route is widened (R117), `su IS NULL вҮ’ permit` means one forgotten seam hands a HOUSEMASTER the whole register; under deny-by-default the same bug yields an empty page. **PR #176 is the proof this is the right call** вҖ” that leak was permit-by-default meeting an unset GUC. Seam: `withStaffScope(schoolId, userId, fn)` wrapping **reads and writes**. Verifier: `scripts/verify-sickbay-grant-boundary.ts` cloned from the parent one, every probe as `omnischools_app`. `parent_deny` is catalog-driven so all four tables are parent-denied free вҖ” **verify, don't assume.**
- **R113 рҹ”ҙ the reader's row filter uses the SAME function the policy uses вҖ” REQUIRED, not belt-and-braces.** A naive `EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM sickbay_chronic_grant вҖҰ)` **breaks**: RLS applies to tables in the reader's own subquery and the grant table is clinical-reader-only (R122), so a grantee's `EXISTS` returns false and he sees nothing. One predicate, two enforcement points, zero divergence. Never over-fetch-then-filter-in-TS; never a per-row `hasGrant` (R68's N+1).
- **R114** expiry/revocation evaluated server-side, per request, in the transaction, against the DB's `now()` вҖ” never a session claim, never middleware. R68's pinned `now` governs **rendering** only. **R115** the coarse role check stays but changes meaning: first statement is `isStaff(roles)` (non-staff вҶ’ `null`, zero SQL), then **exactly one bounded query** returning zero rows for an unentitled staffer. **рҹ”ҙ R116** the Headmaster's default read does NOT extend to `MENTAL_HEALTH` вҖ” structural, inside `chronic_entry_ids`, so his SQL cannot return the row whatever the reader does. Decisive ground: **he is the school's disciplinary authority**, and a psychiatric history in his default read is the exact adjacency that makes an adolescent not disclose вҖ” a register nobody discloses to is worse than no register. **Counts are reader-dependent and R74's partition invariant is evaluated per reader.** **рҹ”ҙ R117 THE ROUTE вҖ” decided, not discovered:** `SICKBAY_ROLES` is **NOT** widened (that would hand HOUSEMASTER the setup page and the today board вҖ” names, beds, complaints no grant covers); the register gets its own wider gate (`requireSchool()` + `isStaff()` + `schoolType !== 'BASIC'`) and **the reader's gate is the only clinical boundary**. A separate grantee route would make a URL a membership oracle. **R118** the detail route returns `notFound()` **indistinguishably** for "no such student" and "no entry you may see" вҖ” membership of the register is itself medical information; no forbidden panel, no distinguishable timing, no different copy. **R119** `getSickbayBoard(schoolId, actor, now)` with `actor: {userId, roles}` вҖ” the field is `userId` not `id` (Sarah's ADV-2 proved an ambiguous identity field name is what lets a tier collapse silently). **R120** the client boundary takes scalars or a separately-pinned view type, **never a reader row** вҖ” вҡ пёҸ this is the increment where 22c's B4 served-HTML half becomes load-bearing.

**D В· read-audit** вҖ” **R121** detail opens only, deduped per (actor Г— entry Г— civil day), in its **own** table `sickbay_chronic_read` with `UNIQUE(...)` + `ON CONFLICT DO NOTHING`: one insert, no read-before-write, no race. Rejected `actionType='viewed'` on `audit_log` (dedupe becomes SELECT-then-INSERT needing a five-column index on a hot shared table вҖ” Risk 3's *"an audit table outgrowing the data"*), and decisively: a separate table can be aged out on its own retention schedule. Fires on the detail route and the dorm-card print; **never** on the list, marker, counters, tiles or a revalidation. **The matron's own opens ARE audited.** В§04's trail is the union of this table and `audit_log`, rendered as one list. **рҹ”ҙ R122** the audit row stores IDs and a scope вҖ” **never a condition string** (the surface's `viewed Esi Antwi В· diabetic protocol` is a leak by proxy on the very screen meant for oversight); and **В§04 is clinical-reader-only** вҖ” a grantee must never learn who *else* knows.

**E В· what 23 owes 22** вҖ” **R123** the queue's chronic column returns as a **neutral boolean marker** `Care plan on file`, rendered only when the actor may read вүҘ1 active entry, **nothing at all** otherwise; R61's false negative (`No chronic flag` asserting *safety* about a register the reader may not fully see) is retired. `SickbayQueueRow` gains exactly ONE key, `hasCarePlan: boolean` вҖ” structurally incapable of naming a condition; the other three row types gain **nothing**. The marker is computed from the entries **the actor may read**, so a Headmaster gets none for a mental-health-only student (a marker he cannot act on is an invitation to ask *"what plan?"*, which is the disclosure). **R124** the visit record's header gains the readable condition chip(s) + a working `View care plan вҶ’`; the SCD protocol **banner** stays omitted (A4: it leaks twice, by name *and* by drug вҖ” `hydroxyurea вҮ’ sickle cell`; a link leaks neither). **R125** В§01 `Last visit` renders timestamp + relative age only вҖ” the reason fragment is omitted (R76/A12 refused this on a *retrospective* log; here it would sit in the same row as a named condition pill, strictly worse) and is unbacked anyway.

**F В· adjacency, ruled fresh** вҖ” **R126 the register's threat model is the GRANTEE, not the shoulder.** On `today` the reader was always a clinician and the risk was who stood behind her; here the reader may be a sports master and the risk is *what he is handed*. So the discipline inverts: **full clinical detail on В§02 is correct and is the surface's purpose** for a `FULL_PLAN` reader, and the whole discipline lives in the per-scope column projection (R98 makes that a fixed key-set). **22c's rulings are NOT re-litigated from this surface.** Never leaking back: no condition/family/pill/drug/membership on `today` beyond R123's boolean В· **a grantee never sees the В§01 list** (his register contains only his granted entries вҖ” falls out of R113 but is an AC in its own right, because "show him the list, gate the detail" is the obvious wrong shortcut) В· drug names never leave В§02 В· no grant metadata to grantees В· `attendance_record.note` stays `null` В· preserve verbatim *"Do not display in dorm common area вҖ” medical privacy applies."* and *"Class teachers see 'M' not 'A'."*

**G В· omit-not-fake at 23 (R127)** вҖ” absent entirely, no shell/badge/anchor/inert button: **all NHIS** (D3 stands, shape at 25) В· **`Open VLC case` + the DMHU visit-log card** (VLC unbuilt; ship `referral_managed` + external-care text columns and no link; `VLC Case 2024-VLC-0047` is a matron-typed string inside `external_pastoral_home`, not a join) В· **`Export PDF` / `Export grant log` / `Export 30-day log`** (the highest-value exfiltration path in the product, no ruling behind it вҖ” E17) В· `Deputy Head (Welfare)` / `School Nurse` as default readers (neither role exists) В· the `Senior prefect` grant row В· the `13:00` column В· the `Last visit` reason fragment В· the five numbered protocol cards *as structure*. Sub-nav is `Today В· Chronic register В· Setup` only. **The demo six must be REAL** вҖ” seeded against seeded students and the six seeded Houses (`AggreyВ·GuggisbergВ·FraserВ·SlessorВ·KingsleyВ·Aryee`; `Kufuor`/`Nkrumah` are drift), and the seeded `Abena Mensah` is renamed **`Adwoa Mensa`** (one string, and it makes the canonical cross-surface demo case real on four surfaces at once).

### AC for Quinn (INCR-23)
- **X1вҖ“X16 + X-MUT В· the boundary verifier**, mechanism cloned from `verify-parent-boundary.ts` (fixtures as superuser in a **rolled-back** tx; every probe after `set local role omnischools_app`). **X1 is the clause that differs from `parent_scope`** вҖ” school GUC set, staff GUC unset вҮ’ **0 rows on all four tables**, and it must go RED if the polarity is flipped to `su IS NULL OR вҖҰ`. X3 Headmaster reads exactly the non-`MENTAL_HEALTH` entries (positive control: the SCD entry and its meds visible). X7 expiry evaluated in the same statement. X9 house-tied grant dies when the student moves House. X10/X11 a grantee cannot extend or self-issue a grant. X12 row relocation refused in **both** directions. X14 **drift guard**: every table in `CHRONIC_TABLES` has both a `staff_grant_scope` and a `parent_deny` policy in `pg_policy`, and the list equals the `sickbay_chronic_*` set exported from `db/schema/sickbay.ts` so a fifth table at 24вҖ“28 cannot escape silently. X15 `withoutTenantScope` is the **only** escape. **X-MUT:** rewriting the function to ignore `su` turns X3/X5/X6/X7/X8/X9 red; dropping the `MENTAL_HEALTH` clause turns **X3 alone** red while X5/X6 stay green вҖ” the asymmetry proves the carve-out is live independently of the grant arm (the 22c ADV-1 proof shape).
- **E1вҖ“E9 entry model** (E3 the CHECK proven with raw SQL, not only through the action В· E6 slot ids **stable across a reset**, proven by comparing before/after В· E9 the `diagnos` sweep).
- **S1вҖ“S6 scope projection** вҖ” S2 `PARTIAL` proven by `Object.keys()` that the clinical columns are **absent, not empty**, with the matron's read of the same row as positive control; S3 `DIRECTIVE` frozen key-set (no condition value, label, pill class or colour token); S5 byte-identical `notFound()`; **S6 adding a clinical column to the `PARTIAL` projection without rendering it turns the runtime key-set pin RED** (the allowlist generalises where a denylist would not).
- **G1вҖ“G5 grants** (G2 proven through a direct POST, not only the UI). **A1вҖ“A6 read-audit** (A2 zero rows across a full 30-entry render; A3 concurrency handled by the UNIQUE, not a check; A5 the matron's own opens audited). **R1вҖ“R5 route & reader** (R2 `SICKBAY_ROLES` unchanged, grep-pinned, with the full 21/22 suites passing untouched В· R3 **statement**-level flatness 6вҶ’30 В· R5 the clinical-gate **expression** pin, RED when the gate is deleted). **D1вҖ“D5 debts to 22.** **O1вҖ“O5 structural** (O1 the from-empty replay with `*_tenant_uk` before the composite FKs вҖ” manual, this repo has no CI).

### OQ1 вҶ’ Wells (answer before writing DDL)
1. Grant scope: third enum vs `text` + CHECK вҖ” defensible either way, Wells's call. 2. `*_tenant_uk` inline in `CREATE TABLE` as 0057 did (0033 hazard). 3. Does `SECURITY DEFINER STABLE` taking `school_id` **from the row** force per-row evaluation under `withSchool`? If so, re-shape it to take a constant. 4. Confirm the `app.bypass_rls` arm is syntactically identical to `tenant_isolation`'s and that seeds/`db:policies`/`withoutTenantScope` still pass. 5. The three CHECKs (`MENTAL_HEALTH вҮ’ NOT on_site_treatable AND referral_managed` В· `is_prn XOR slot_id` В· `DIRECTIVE вҮ’ directive_note NOT NULL`). 6. вҡ пёҸ the grant partial-unique **cannot** use `now()` (not immutable) вҖ” fall back to `WHERE revoked_at IS NULL`, expiry in the reader. 7. `slot_id` composite FK RESTRICT (this is what forces R100 into 23a). 8. `read_on` as `date`, Africa/Accra civil date from `civilDate()`. 9. `prod-paste-0058-sickbay-chronic.sql` = DDL + the four policies + the function, **and** the catalog-driven `parent_deny` loop re-run (or the four new tables are parent-readable on prod until someone runs `db:policies`).

### INCR-23a В· Wells вҖ” migration 0058 + the third boundary (commit `bfae974`, pushed to `senior-feat`)
Files: `db/schema/sickbay.ts` В· `db/schema/_enums.ts` В· `db/migrations/0058_windy_silver_sable.sql` В· `db/sql/policies.sql` В· **`db/sql/prod-paste-0058-sickbay-chronic.sql`** В· `lib/db/rls.ts` (`withStaffScope`).

**OQ1 answered вҖ” two of the nine corrected the spec:**
1. **Grant scope IS an enum** (`sickbay_grant_scope`, module-prefixed) вҖ” what BUILD_STACK L350 already declares, the idiom of all 8 shipped 4.4 enums, and it hands the implementer a real TS union (a `text`+CHECK column infers as `string`). **So 0058 is 3 enums + 4 tables, not R93's 2 + 4** вҖ” the only count that moved, and OQ1 #1 delegated it.
2. Tenant UKs inline in `CREATE TABLE`; all four tables emitted before any `ADD FOREIGN KEY`. Verified by **reading the emitted SQL**, not by exit code. Three composite FKs consume the entry UK in this same file вҖ” the 0033 hazard, closed.
3. **рҹ”ҙ CORRECTED вҖ” the correlated form is a real O(nВІ) cliff, proven by EXPLAIN both ways.** Passing `school_id` **from the row** gives a plain `(SubPlan 1)`, re-executed per row, each execution scanning the entry table whose own policy re-runs the predicate per entry. Passing the **GUC constant** gives `(hashed SubPlan 2)` вҖ” built once, probed per row. So every policy passes `NULLIF(current_setting('app.current_school',true),'')::uuid`, never `school_id`. Equivalent because `tenant_isolation` already forces `school_id =` that GUC on any row that can survive. **A deliberate divergence from `parent_student_ids(school_id, pu)`, which is correlated today** вҖ” worth revisiting there.
4. `app.bypass_rls` arm byte-identical to `tenant_isolation`'s and verified: a bypass-shaped session reads 2/1/3 with both other GUCs empty. `db:policies`, `db:rls-test`, `verify-parent-boundary` (89 deny tables, zero leaks) all green.
5. All three CHECKs ship and were proven **with raw SQL, not through an action**, rejecting both directions with positive controls.
6. **рҹ”ҙ CORRECTED вҖ” the recommended `WHERE revoked_at IS NULL` fallback is WRONG, and no live-grant unique shipped.** An **expired grant is not a revoked one**, so a July dead-but-unrevoked row would reject August's lawful re-grant with a unique violation, and the only workaround is stamping `revoked_at` on something that merely expired вҖ” **a lie inside a clinical audit trail** (R110). It also buys nothing: duplicate live grants are semantically idempotent (both matron-issued, no escalation), and the reader must resolve a *set* of live grants regardless (an expired `FULL_PLAN` beside a live `DIRECTIVE` must collapse to `DIRECTIVE` whatever an index says). вҡ пёҸ **23b owes the precedence rule** вҖ” which scope wins when two live grants exist on one entry (Wells recommends widest-wins; with Kofi).
7. `slot_id` composite FK RESTRICT **+ an index on `(school_id, slot_id)`** вҖ” Postgres does not index FKs, and an unindexed RESTRICT target means a seq scan of every prescription in the school on every schedule edit. **R100 is now a HARD BLOCKER, not a nice-to-have: `resetScheduleSlots` hard-DELETEs slot rows, so after 0058 "Reset to defaults" ERRORS for any school with a med schedule.** Must become a reconcile in this same release.
8. `read_on date NOT NULL` from the shipped `civilDate()`; it is the dedupe key and a timestamp cannot be one.
9. Prod paste ends with the verbatim catalog-driven `parent_deny` loop + a рҹ”ҙ note on skipping it.

**Deviations from Kofi's spec, each forced and each reported:**
- **рҹ”ҙ THREE `SECURITY DEFINER` functions, not one.** SECURITY DEFINER does **not** exempt you from `FORCE` RLS, so a single `chronic_entry_ids` called from the entry table's own policy reads that table вҶ’ re-enters the policy вҶ’ calls itself вҶ’ **infinite recursion at runtime**. The acyclic fix: `chronic_clinical_role(school,su) вҶ’ text` (must be DEFINER вҖ” it joins the **global `ref_role`**, which has bare ENABLE and no policy, so a non-owner session reads zero rows and an inline join would silently evaluate to "no role" for the very session it authorises) вҶ’ `chronic_entry_readable(school,su,entry,student,cond) вҶ’ boolean`, **the** predicate, taking id/student/condition as *arguments* precisely so it never reads the entry table вҶ’ `chronic_entry_ids(school,su) вҶ’ SETOF uuid`, its projection, and the signature R113 requires the reader to call. **X-MUT still discriminates as specified.**
- **рҹ”ҙ One place the DB is coarser than R116, cycle-forced.** The grant policy cannot read the entry table (`entry вҶ’ grant вҶ’ entry`), so its rule is "a default clinical reader OR your own grant row" вҖ” and a HEADMASTER is a default clinical reader. **вҡ пёҸ Wells characterised the residue as harmless ("no student, no name, no condition"); that is wrong** вҖ” the grant row carries `scope_label`, `reason` and `directive_note`, all matron-authored free text, and R109 makes `directive_note` deliberately clinical-adjacent. A Headmaster barred from a `MENTAL_HEALTH` entry can read a grant row against it, **learn a sixth entry exists** (which R116 forbids) and read prose that may name the condition. **Open with Kofi (product) and Sarah (security).**
- **The grantee CAN read his own grant row вҖ” required, not a courtesy.** `chronic_entry_readable` reads the grant table to evaluate entitlement, so a blanket clinical-only rule there makes **every grant self-defeating**. Own-row-only is the shipped `student_guardian`/`parent_scope` idiom, and R122's "never learn who *else* knows" is preserved.
- **Asymmetric USING / WITH CHECK on the entry table вҖ” mandatory.** A `WITH CHECK` is evaluated on a row that does not exist yet, so any "an entry you may read" write rule is FALSE for every INSERT and **no matron could ever create a care plan**. Write rules are actor-shaped (`chronic_clinical_role IS NOT NULL`), which also stops a FULL_PLAN grantee editing the plan or injecting a dose. On `sickbay_chronic_read` the asymmetry inverts (everyone WITH-CHECKs their own row in, only clinical readers USING-read the trail) вҖ” which makes the trail append-only against a grantee. вҡ пёҸ **the audit insert must not use `.returning()`** (RETURNING needs SELECT).
- **Three extra `staff_grant_delete` policies (FOR DELETE, RESTRICTIVE).** DELETE is authorised by USING alone, so without them a FULL_PLAN grantee could **delete the care plan he was shown**, and any grantee could delete his own grant row and **erase the evidence he ever had access**.
- **`OTHER` exempt from the per-condition partial unique** вҖ” it is R94's escape hatch, so capping a student at one `OTHER` row caps the register (coeliac *and* hypertension is legitimate).
- Five of Lucy's N17 columns not shipped (unruled by Kofi, each replaceable): `goal_signal`, `scope_limits`, `protocol_title`, and `superseded_at`/`superseded_by` (R103 kills those two outright).

**Verified on dev as `omnischools_app` via `SET LOCAL ROLE`, rolled back:** school GUC set + **staff GUC unset вҶ’ 0/0/0/0** (flip the polarity to `su IS NULL OR` and it becomes 2/1/3) В· MATRON 2/1/3 В· **HEADMASTER 1 entry, `SICKLE_CELL` only** В· FULL_PLAN grantee 1/1/1-own-grant/0-audit В· self-issue refused, expiry-extension refused, all three DELETEs 0 rows, entry UPDATE refused, **matron positive control passes all four** В· house-tied grant 1 вҶ’ 0 on House move вҶ’ 1 on return В· expired DIRECTIVE grantee 0 В· matron of A scoped to B 0 В· bypass 2/1/3. `tsc` clean, 668/668.

**вҡ пёҸ `db:push` is unusable on this dev DB** вҖ” it demands truncating `boarding_infractions` to add a pre-existing missing `boarding_infractions_tenant_uk` (unrelated drift, destroys 10 rows). 0058 was applied via `docker psql --single-transaction`, then `db:policies`, then the prod paste replayed over the top to prove idempotency (catalog unchanged: 15 policies / 15 FKs / 4 uniques / 3 CHECKs). **That drift needs its own ticket.**

**рҹ”ҙ PROD DEPLOY REQUIRED вҖ” `db/sql/prod-paste-0058-sickbay-chronic.sql`**, one idempotent paste: enums вҶ’ 4 tables вҶ’ FKs вҶ’ indexes вҶ’ ENABLE/FORCE/`tenant_isolation` вҶ’ the 3 helpers вҶ’ 4 `staff_grant_scope` + 3 `staff_grant_delete` вҶ’ **the `parent_deny` loop re-run**. Then `db/sql/verify-prod-rls.sql` (Query 1 zero rows; tenant_tables +4; parent_denied +4) and the header's `pg_policy` query вҖ” expect exactly 15 rows. **Skipping the paste does not leak a bed count: R117 opens the route to all staff and the RLS is the only clinical boundary, so it hands a school's adolescent mental-health register to whoever logs in next.**

**Still owed before 23a can ship:** R100 `resetScheduleSlots` reconcile (now hard-fails) В· `scripts/verify-sickbay-grant-boundary.ts` (X1вҖ“X16 вҖ” Wells's probes were throwaway scratchpad SQL, not a repo file) В· the reader must call `chronic_entry_ids` (a hand-written `EXISTS` on the grant table fails closed and confusingly) В· 23b's multiple-live-grant precedence В· В§04 must INNER JOIN the entry.

### INCR-23a В· Kofi R128вҖ“R131 + Sarah's security read on `bfae974` вҖ” рҹ”ҙ 23a IS BLOCKED, and one finding outranks the increment

**рҹ”ҙрҹ”ҙ CRITICAL вҖ” `assignStaffRole` (and nine siblings) have NO role gate. Live on `main`. Paused 23a to hotfix it.**
Every exported mutator in `lib/actions/staff.ts` вҖ” `addStaff`, `importStaff`, `saveStaffProfile`, `updateStaff`, `deleteStaff`, `deleteStaffBulk`, **`assignStaffRole`**, `removeStaffRole`, `saveStaffCompensation` вҖ” is gated by `requireSchool()` alone, which **since PR #176 means "authenticated + is staff" and nothing more**. `ADMIN` is in `STAFF_ROLES` (`lib/staff-roles.ts:9`) and `components/staff/staff-row.tsx:128` renders the role editor for every row. **So any teacher, librarian or sports master can open `/staff`, find their own row and assign themselves `ADMIN` вҖ” three clicks, no crafted request.** Sarah found it as self-promotion to `MATRON` (which defeats this increment's entire boundary, since `chronic_clinical_role` reads `role_assignment`); the wider truth is full administrative takeover of the tenant, plus bulk staff deletion and write access to payroll via `saveStaffCompensation`.
**Root cause is the same seam as #176, one layer up:** #176 correctly made `requireSchool()` mean *is staff*; a **role-management** surface needs *is an administrator*, and nothing supplies it. The escalation is audit-logged (`recordAudit вҖҰ "Role assigned"`), so it is detectable after the fact вҖ” that is the only mitigation present. **The third boundary is keyed on a table its own subjects can write.** Hotfix off `main`, then resume.

**Kofi R128 вҖ” the grant-row residue is a VIOLATION of R116/E18, not residue.** Wells's *"no student, no name, no condition"* is true only of the column list read literally. Three grounds: (1) **existence** вҖ” a grant row carries `entry_id`, so a Headmaster whose `chronic_entry_ids` returns 5, holding a grant row whose `entry_id` is in none of them, has been handed the signal *by construction and can count them*; that is the literal negation of the sentence the owner ratified in E18. (2) **Free-text clinical payload** вҖ” `chronic_grant_directive_needs_note` *forces* `directive_note` non-null for every DIRECTIVE grant and R109 defines it as the grantee's entire operational view of the child, so the column cannot be assumed condition-free; `reason` is by definition the matron's justification. **This is R122's family** вҖ” R122 refused a condition string on a row already carrying `entry_id + actor + scope`, and there is no principled reading under which a stored enum is a disclosure but a stored sentence about the same entry is not. (3) **The adjacency R116 was ruled FOR** вҖ” `grantee_user_id + house_id + granted_at` tells the disciplinary authority which HM was recently briefed about a boy in his House; the entry is not needed. Scope: **only** the grant table has the hole; `_med` and `_read` gate on `entry_id IN chronic_entry_ids(...)` and are correct as shipped.
- **Kofi R129 вҖ” close it with an FK-pinned policy BIT, not the condition, not MATRON-only, not an app-layer strip.** The cycle is real and stands (any grant policy reading the entry table recurses; Postgres does not guarantee OR short-circuit across policy arms, so the loop is a planner decision, not a guarantee). **Required outcome:** a HEADMASTER selecting from `sickbay_chronic_grant` gets **zero rows** whose entry his default read excludes, evaluated **inside the RLS predicate**, with **no read of the entry table**, and the stored discriminator must be **incapable of diverging** without a loud failure. Recommended shape: `sickbay_chronic_entry.hm_restricted boolean GENERATED ALWAYS AS (condition = 'MENTAL_HEALTH') STORED` + `UNIQUE (school_id, id, hm_restricted)`; `sickbay_chronic_grant.hm_restricted boolean NOT NULL` with the entry FK becoming composite `(school_id, entry_id, hm_restricted)` **`ON UPDATE CASCADE`**. **Why not a plain insert-time boolean: it fails OPEN on re-classification** (a grant stamped `false` against an entry later corrected to `MENTAL_HEALTH` stays Headmaster-visible) вҖ” the dangerous direction, and R94's own вҡ пёҸ concedes re-classification happens. Under CASCADE the DB propagates the flip and a wrong stamp is an **FK violation at INSERT, not a silent leak** вҖ” which answers R10 squarely (R10 forbids a stored value that *can* disagree). Named for the policy fact, not the diagnosis, so the string `MENTAL_HEALTH` never lands on a grant row. Fallback if Postgres refuses the shape: plain NOT NULL boolean **plus** `condition` immutable after insert (mis-classification corrected by `active = false` + a new entry, which the R91 partial unique already permits and which correctly drops every stale grant). **Timing:** the grant table is empty until 23b's `grantAccess`, so no live exposure вҖ” **fold the DDL into 0058 while the PR is open**; if 0058 had already merged and been pasted it becomes 0059 and a hard blocker on 23b.
- **Kofi R130 вҖ” В§04's reader does not change; its STATUS does.** The INNER JOIN to the entry **stays** (R113's "one predicate, two enforcement points"; it also supplies the student and pill В§04 renders), but it stops being the sole enforcement of R116 and becomes defence-in-depth. **New AC:** deleting the reader's INNER JOIN must still return zero grant rows for a HEADMASTER on a granted `MENTAL_HEALTH` entry, **and** flipping the policy arm back to `IS NOT NULL` must turn that probe RED while X3 stays green вҖ” two mutations, two independent enforcement points. Add to X14: every `sickbay_chronic_*` `staff_grant_scope` USING must gate on `chronic_entry_ids(...)` **or** carry the `hm_restricted` arm, so a fifth table at 24вҖ“28 cannot inherit the coarse rule by copy-paste.
- **Kofi R131 вҖ” widest-wins, confirmed, four bindings.** No live-grant unique (Wells's reasoning adopted verbatim вҖ” forcing `revoked_at` on a merely-expired grant is a false statement in a clinical audit trail, dispositive on its own). Widest-wins because every live grant is a MATRON's explicit authorisation and narrowest-wins makes her most recent act a silent no-op. (1) the set is **live** grants only, per R114's DB `now()` in the same statement; (2) total order `FULL_PLAN > PARTIAL > DIRECTIVE` and the projection is **the winner's key-set, never a union** (a merged key-set is a fourth unpinned scope and defeats S6); (3) the read-audit records the winning scope at the **first** audited open of the day and must **not** become an upsert (`DO UPDATE` needs SELECT/UPDATE on a table a grantee cannot read вҖ” the same reason `.returning()` is banned); (4) **В§04 lists every live grant and the effective scope, not just the winner** вҖ” otherwise a matron revokes the DIRECTIVE row, access persists via a live FULL_PLAN, and the surface has lied about the consequence of her own action.

**рҹ”ҙ Sarah HIGH-1 вҖ” the write rules are wider than the ruling, and Kofi found it independently.** All three `WITH CHECK`s and the `staff_grant_delete` loop test `chronic_clinical_role(...) IS NOT NULL` = *MATRON or HEADMASTER*, where **R39** says clinical write is MATRON-only and **R111** says grant/revoke is MATRON-only. `USING` is the read predicate; **an INSERT never touches `USING`**. вң… Sarah verified the exploit as `omnischools_app`: as HEADMASTER, `select count(*) вҖҰ MENTAL_HEALTH` вҶ’ 0, then one `INSERT INTO sickbay_chronic_grant вҖҰ select вҖҰ FROM sickbay_chronic_grant WHERE scope='DIRECTIVE'` naming himself вҶ’ then reads the entry, `condition_detail`, `emergency_protocol` and **Sertraline**. **He obtained the `entry_id` from the grant table itself вҖ” so R128's residue is not decoration, it is the enumeration step of this escalation.** Same root cause also lets a HEADMASTER author/edit care plans and doses (R39 bypass) and un-revoke, extend, re-target or **delete** any grant (R110/R111 bypass вҖ” the append-only trail is app-layer-only against him). **Fix: one token, four places, in BOTH `policies.sql` and the prod paste** вҖ” `chronic_clinical_role(...) = 'MATRON'`. Nothing legitimate breaks (the helper already prefers `'MATRON'` when a user holds both; seeds/ETL run under bypass).
**рҹ”ҙ Sarah HIGH-2 вҖ” the residue confirmed and extended** (see R128). Her cycle-free alternative if the prose must go: move `scope_label`/`reason`/`directive_note` to a child `sickbay_chronic_grant_note` policed by `entry_id IN chronic_entry_ids(...)` вҖ” nothing reads that table, so the graph stays acyclic. **Column privileges do NOT work: the app connects as the table owner on prod and column grants do not bind the owner.** With HIGH-1 fixed the residue drops to a bounded read-side prose leak and is no longer an escalation.
**рҹҹ  Sarah MEDIUM-1 вҖ” the read audit is forgeable AND suppressible.** вң… Verified: `sickbay_chronic_read`'s `WITH CHECK` never checks `actor_user_id` is the session, so a FULL_PLAN grantee inserted a row **attributed to the HEADMASTER** (and `actor_user_id` FKs the **global** `ref_user`, so the forged actor need not even be in this school). He cannot read the trail back вҖ” **he writes into an oversight log he cannot see**, the worst asymmetry for В§04's credibility. Second: **`scope` is not in the dedupe key**, so a grantee can pre-insert tomorrow's row with the narrowest scope and the genuine `FULL_PLAN` insert silently no-ops, permanently understating what he was shown. Fix: `AND actor_user_id = <the staff GUC>` in `WITH CHECK`; plus restrictive `FOR UPDATE`/`FOR DELETE USING (bypass)` so a **matron cannot delete the audit of her own opens** вҖ” the one thing В§04 exists to prevent. вң… The `.returning()` footgun **fails CLOSED, loudly** (RLS violation aborts the tx) вҖ” the residual risk is an implementer wrapping it in `try/catch`, which serves the read **unaudited**.
**рҹҹ  Sarah MEDIUM-2 вҖ” `SET search_path = public` is exploitable; `pg_temp` shadowing promotes anyone to MATRON.** вң… Verified end-to-end: as a TEACHER, `create temp table role_assignment/ref_role`, insert a fake MATRON row, and `chronic_clinical_role()` flips `NULL вҶ’ 'MATRON'`, entries `1 вҶ’ 3`, both drug names visible. Postgres searches the temp schema first for **relations** when `pg_temp` is not named explicitly. Precondition is arbitrary session SQL вҖ” defence-in-depth вҖ” **but RLS is precisely the layer that must survive an injection.** вң… Fix verified: `SET search_path = public, pg_temp` on all three helpers **and on the shipped `parent_student_ids`, which has the same flaw.**
**рҹҹ  Sarah MEDIUM-3 вҖ” the DB boundary is entry-level and scope-blind; R109's "structurally incapable of leaking" is APP-LAYER ONLY.** вң… Verified: the DIRECTIVE-only TEACHER selects the whole entry row вҖ” `MENTAL_HEALTH`, `bereavement, self-harm risk`, `Escalate to DMHU` вҖ” and `Sertraline 50mg ON`. RLS is row-level and cannot mask columns (already stated at `policies.sql:344-346`). Not fixable at the DB layer without column policies, so **this must be the loudest line in the 23b handoff: S2/S3's key-set pins are load-bearing security controls, not tidiness**, and `select *` or spreading a reader row into a client component is a direct disclosure of exactly the tier R109 exists to prevent.
**рҹҹ  Sarah MEDIUM-4 вҖ” `verify-prod-rls.sql` cannot see the third boundary.** It checks tenant isolation, the parent boundary and global tables. If the operator pastes the DDL and both loops but the `staff_grant_scope` block fails or is skipped, **Query 1 returns ZERO ROWS = PASS while every staff member reads the whole register** (R117 opens the route to all staff; the reader's gate is the only clinical boundary). Add a **check D** in the file's own doctrine: every `sickbay_chronic_%` table must carry a **restrictive** `staff_grant_scope`, and entry/med/grant a `staff_grant_delete`. That is the durable version of X14 and the only thing that catches a fifth chronic table at 24вҖ“28 escaping on prod.
- **вң… Sarah corrected the prod paste's own warning.** Skipping the trailing `parent_deny` loop does **NOT** leave the tables parent-readable (verified: staff GUC unset вҶ’ 0 rows on all four, and a parent session never sets it) вҖ” `staff_grant_scope`'s deny-by-default already covers it. The real costs are that check B goes red (the *good* outcome) and the defence-in-depth layer is gone. **The overstated warning must be corrected вҖ” a warning that is demonstrably wrong is the kind that gets ignored the third time.**
- **рҹҹЎ L1 вҖ” dev proves LESS than prod inside a SECURITY DEFINER.** The helpers are owned by `omnischools` (`rolsuper = t`), so on dev their bodies bypass RLS entirely: with **no GUCs at all**, `omnischools_app` called `chronic_entry_ids(A, <matron>)` вҶ’ 3 ids вҖ” a full cross-tenant oracle. вң… It closes on prod (re-run under `CREATE ROLE probe_owner NOSUPERUSER` ownership вҶ’ 0 ids, NULL, NULL). **Quinn must not build an AC on a direct helper call.** **рҹҹЎ L2 вҖ” the three-function graph is genuinely acyclic**, verified empirically under prod-shaped ownership with identical numbers and no recursion. It terminates because the grant policy reads only `role_assignment`; **`ref_role`'s bare ENABLE (no FORCE) is what keeps `chronic_clinical_role` correct on prod**, so a future FORCE on `ref_role` would silently make every clinical reader a nobody. Standing invariant: any policy added to `students`/`house`/`role_assignment`/`ref_role`/`sickbay_chronic_grant` that reads a `sickbay_chronic_*` table closes the cycle вҖ” **23b is the near-term temptation and does not need one.** **рҹҹЎ L3** helper EXECUTE is PUBLIC (PostgREST RPC on Supabase) вҖ” returns nothing without the GUCs, so hardening not a hole; REVOKE anyway. **рҹҹЎ L4** the bypass arm is byte-identical and not a wider door, but on these tables it satisfies both families вҖ” **treat a chronic table inside `withoutTenantScope` as an automatic review trigger** (it reads every school and writes no audit row). **рҹҹЎ L5** `withStaffScope` hygiene correct вҖ” every `set_config` is `is_local = true`, `userId` bound as a parameter; a `withSchool` nested inside takes a different pooled connection with no staff GUC, which under this polarity yields an empty page, not a leak. **рҹ”ҙ L6 вҖ” one query to run on prod, once: `select rolbypassrls from pg_roles where rolname = current_user;`** The repo asserts Supabase's `postgres` lacks BYPASSRLS (`policies.sql:9-11`) and every FORCE-RLS guarantee depends on it; **it has never been confirmed. If it is true, none of 0055вҖ“0058 is enforced on prod.**

**Sarah's blocking list for the 23a PR when it opens:** CRITICAL-1, HIGH-1, MEDIUM-1, MEDIUM-2, MEDIUM-4. HIGH-2 is Kofi's call (now ruled: close it via R129). MEDIUM-3 is not DB-fixable and becomes the 23b handoff's loudest instruction. **The prod paste must be re-pasted after the policy corrections land, since it duplicates the policy text in `policies.sql` and the two drift independently.**
